may concurrently serve an administrative notice to abate a public nuisance upon the owner or occupant and demand that compliance must be achieved within seven consecutive days after service of the notice not including the date of receipt or posting b the town shall determine the individual firm or corporation or lien holder who from the records in the county tax assessors office it appears to be the titled owner or lien holder of the property and cause a written notice of public notice to be served on such individual firm or corporation or lien holder by 1 personal service as attested to by affidavit of service  or by 2 copy mailed to such owner or lien holder at such place or address by united states certified mail return receipt requested 3 after due diligence if service is unable to be perfected as described above the town shall cause a copy of the aforesaid notice to be posted at such structure location or premises which shall serve as notice to the public c the notice to abate the nuisance shall inform the person of the specific nuisances with citation to this section provide names numbers and addresses for contact with the town  inform them of their rights to an appeal and that upon the eighth day after receipt of service or posting the town may abate the condition and assess an administrative fee and all public costs as a lien against the property d that in the event the town shall seek to demolish or remove a structure other than a dwelling as the word is defined in section 83 of the town then the due process provisions of section 81 et seq shall be followed in any action brought by the town as to said structure appeal proceedings  hearing a appeal of finding of nuisance the responsible person owner or occupant or the lien holder of the property may make a written demand to the town administrator for a hearing on the question of whether a public nuisance in fact exists this appeal stays the public abatement until such time as the matter is heard and decided by the board of adjustments and appeals the appeal must be received by the administrator within five business days of the posting or appellants receipt of the notice to abate excluding town recognized holidays and weekends the written demand shall include an address contact number either phone or facsimile in order for the person to be informed of the hearing location date and time it shall not be a defense to the determination that a public nuisance exists that the property is boarded up or otherwise enclosed the board may amend or modify the notice to abate the public nuisance or when appropriate under the facts presented extend the time for compliance by the owner to such date as the majority of the appeals board may determine the decisions of the board are final and shall be delivered orally to the appellant on the date of the hearing and such decision shall be written and mailed to the address provided b failure to appeal failure to appeal constitutes waiver of the right to appeal the existence of a public nuisance c appeal of assessment further in those instances where the nuisance has been abated by the town after the required notice of subsection 127b the owner or occupant of the property who has been served with a notice of assessment pursuant to section 129 of this chapter may make a written demand to the administrator for a hearing to review the cost of the abatement this appeal stays the attachment of the lien until such time as the matter is heard and decided by the hearing board the appeal of the assessment must be received by the administrator within five business days of the appellants receipt of the notice of assessment the written demand shall include an address contact number either phone or facsimile in order for the person to be informed of the hearing location date and time in an appeal of the assessment of costs no testimony shall be permitted on the issue of the existence of the public nuisance the decisions of the board are final and shall be delivered orally to the appellant on the date of the hearing and such decision shall be written and mailed to the address provided d failure to appeal assessment failure to timely appeal constitutes a waiver of the right to appeal the assessment of costs e notice of hearing by way of the address and contact numbers provided in the written demand the administrator shall orally advise the owner of the location date and time of the hearing and shall also advise the person of the hearing in writing mail notice of the hearing must be provided at least two business days prior to the hearing excluding townrecognized holidays and weekends f timing and manner of hearings the hearings as allowed under this section shall be held as soon as practical but in no event later than 20 business days after receipt of the appeal excluding town recognized holidays and weekends the hearing shall be informally conducted by the administrator or designee chief of police or designee and director of public works or designee the enforcement officer shall present the facts and circumstances that resulted in a conclusion that a public nuisance existed the owner occupant or lien holder or their agents representatives or attorneys shall be given the opportunity to present evidence to the appeals board in the course of the hearing and shall have the right of cross examination of the enforcement officer when the nuisance has been abated by the town and the person has appealed the assessment of the administrative fee and actual costs the hearing board shall have discretion to waive the administrative fee or the public cost of abating a nuisance in whole or in part if in the course of the hearing reviewing the decision the hearing board finds that justice and equity require such waiver or that any of the following did not conform to the provisions of this chapter 1 the notice to remove the nuisance  2 the work performed in abating the nuisance  3 the computation of charges liability for costs in the event of refusal or neglect of a person to cause such nuisance to be abated in the manner and within the time provided herein it shall be reported to the administrator who may in a reasonable and prudent manner direct the expenditure of public resources to abate the nuisance condition the cost of the abatement shall include an administrative assessment of $15000 in addition to the actual cost of labor and materials expended in public abatement the person shall be served with a notice of assessment within seven days of the completion of the abatement the notice of assessment shall include the administrative fee and a statement of public costs attested to by affidavit and shall be issued and served as provided for in subsection 127b upon the person responsible for payment who shall make payment within 30 days of the date of service upon the expiration of the 30day period if the amount has not been paid in full or contested before the administrator the administrator may cause a lien in that amount to be filed with the county clerk of court and with the town clerk the lien shall be of record in the county courthouse and the office of the town clerk in the book of liens until paid or recovered or otherwise released collection of the lien by way of recovery or foreclosure may be instituted by the town attorney on behalf of the town or other method available to the town liability of enforcing officers no person carrying out the provisions of this chapter shall be held to answer in any civil or criminal action offensesmiscellaneous consumption of beer wine and alcohol restricted a all provisions and requirements of the general law of the state in regard to beer wine and alcoholic beverages as contained in the alcoholic beverage control act sc laws 197 616 et seq insofar as such provisions can have application within the town are hereby adopted and made a part of this fully as though set out herein all persons within the town shall strictly comply with the regulations by such sections when so applicable b it shall be unlawful for any person to consume beer or wine on the street sidewalk or in lots commonly used by the public for parking within the town unless such location has been approved and licensed as a sidewalk cafe under the towns zoning ordinance and meets all local and state requirements c it shall be unlawful for any person to consume or sell beer wine liquor or other intoxicating beverages in or upon publicly owned streets parking lots sidewalks alleys parks playgrounds or any other publicly owned property within the town of cheraw exceptions to this section will be limited to 1 those business establishments that have obtained the proper permits to operate sidewalk or outdoor cafs 2 events held at the cheraw community center where proper permits relating to alcohol have been obtained    editors note adopted jan 10 201 changed the title of  131 from alcoholic beveragesadoption of state law to consumption of beer wine and alcohol restricted arrestresisting no person shall resist any police officer or other peace officer of the town in making a legal arrest or other discharge of his duty burning grass and rubbish it shall be unlawful for any person to burn or cause to be burned any grass leaves tree limbs trash or rubbish of any kind or description whatsoever within the town whether such grass leaves tree limbs trash or rubbish be located upon private property or upon any of the public streets or alleys of the town without first obtaining permission to do so from the fire chief disturbancesassemblies it shall be unlawful for any person to interrupt or disturb any audience or other lawful assembly of persons within the town limits by any noise loud talking indecent behavior or other such boisterous or annoying behavior or conduct false pretenses  obtaining property or signatures any person who shall by any false pretense or representation obtain the signature of any person to any written instrument or shall obtain from any other person any money valuable security or other property real or personal with intent to defraud or cheat any person of the same shall be punished upon conviction in section 16 of this   provided that this section shall only apply in cases in which the property or item of value so obtained has a value of $100000 or less fireworks see title 23 of the sc laws as amended loitering it shall be unlawful for any person to loiter or congregate on any of the public sidewalks streets or public rightsofway in such a manner as to interfere with or obstruct the free use of the same to the public curfew for juveniles it shall be unlawful for any minor 16 years of age of younger to loiter wander stroll or play in or upon the public streets highways roads alleys parks playgrounds or other public grounds public places vacant lots or other place unsupervised by an adult having the lawful authority to be at such places between the hours of  midnight until  am on the following day  provided that the provisions of this section shall not apply in the following instances 1 when a minor is accompanied by his or her parent legal guardian or other adult person over 21 years of age having the lawful care and custody of the minor  2 when the minor is upon an emergency errand directed by his or her parent or legal guardian or adult person over 21 years of age having the lawful care and custody of the minor  3 when the minor is returning directly home from a civic school or recreational activity  or 4 when a minor is returning directly home form a lawful employment that makes it necessary for him to be in the above referenced places during the prescribed period of time parent guardian or responsible adult  penalty it shall be unlawful for the parent guardian or adult person having custody or control of any child 16 years of age or younger to permit or by insufficient control to allow such child to be in or upon the public streets or any other places listed in section 138 within the town between the hours of  midnight until  am on the following day except in circumstances set out in subsections 1 4 of section 138 upon violation of this section for the first time a person shall be given a warning citation upon conviction of this section a person shall be subject to a fine not to exceed $50000 and costs or imprisonment in jail for not more than 30 days or performance of public service work for the town for not more than 30 days or be subject to any one or more of the stated penalties  subject to all limitations contained in the charter of the town each violation of this section shall constitute a separate offense parades it shall be unlawful for any person to stage any parade or procession on any of the streets or in any other public places within the town without first having applied and secured a special permit from the police chief to do so excepting funeral processions the armed forces of the united states the military forces of this state and the force of the police and fire departments of the town such application shall contain the following information the date and time of such proposed parade or processions  the streets to be used  the number of persons or vehicles to be engaged  and the purpose of such parade or procession upon receipt of such application the police chief shall in his discretion issue such permit subject to the public convenience and public welfare scattering leaflets etc it shall be unlawful for any person to throw or scatter any advertising matter of any nature whatsoever on any street lane alley sidewalk public place or on the premises or vehicle of another without permission of the owner discharging firearms it shall be unlawful for any person to discharge fire or explode any handgun rifle shotgun or other form of firearms in the town limits  provide however that this section shall not be construed to regulate the protection of oneself from immediate dangers to life and limb shooting bows arrows slingshots and missiles the shooting of bows and arrows or the use of slingshots or any other device for throwing missiles within the town is hereby declared to be a nuisance and any person offending shall be liable to a fine or imprisonment for each and every offense false alarms a no person shall make or cause to be made with intent to deceive any false alarm by means of the fire alarm system public or private alarm systems telephone or by any other means of communication b no person shall willfully make or cause to be made any false call for ambulance or rescue service by means of any communication c this section shall not apply to any authorized personnel while installing testing or repairing alarm systems in the normal course of employment penalties for repeated false alarms a any person firm or corporation having a fire alarm smoke detector burglar alarm or other type of alarm and which alarm has a direct or indirect connection which calls for a response from the police or fire department shall be allowed two false alarms during any one calendar year and will be charged a fee of $5000 for the third false alarm responded to by the police or fire department within such calendar year and $20000 for each false alarm responded to thereafter within such calendar year b such fee may be waived if the possessor of the alarm shows to the satisfaction of the police or fire chief that the false alarm was not the result of negligence or improper maintenance damaging public utility poles and signposts no person shall willfully or wantonly injure or break any of the public street lights or any lampposts telephone electric telegraph fire alarm post or any signpost or street sign tampering with property of public utilities  manhole covers a no person shall alter remove molest or tamper with any wire fixture pipe conduit meter or other appliance of the waterworks plant gas electrical cable television or telephone company or person operating a similar business  or tap any supply wires or pipes or fraudulently or secretly extract or use water electricity cable television or gas of the plant or company or uncover or open any manhole of other opening to any sewer unless the person doing so is an authorized employee of the company or the town or under authority and director to do so b no person shall leave any manhole or other opening unprotected or open without replacing the fixtures and appliances in their proper place and position tampering with utility lines and posting bills on utility poles and signs no person shall meddle tamper with injure break cut take down or disarrange any telephone cable television electric light pole fire or police alarm box or pole or any wire cord lamp or other apparatus used in operating or maintaining any utility or alarm system without authority to do so or post any bills signs or posters of any kind whatsoever upon any such poles or posts within the town injury to flowers shrubs fences grass plots etc no person shall willfully and without authority cut pull pluck or otherwise injure any flowers flowering plants shrubs or trees growing in or around any public or private grounds or otherwise injure or destroy any gate fence bench seat bridge building or other structures or property on public property no person shall walk or injure any grass plots planted by the town where prohibitory signs are posted flags and decorations  removing or injuring no person shall remove destroy molest deface or disarrange any flag or other decoration that may be used by any person in upon or about any building to indicate celebration of any holiday or public event within without the consent of the owner damaging monuments and signs no person shall willfully remove destroy mutilate damage or deface in any way or to any extent any monument or sign in on or upon any public park street cemetery or private property of the town injuring public property and property open to the public no person shall willfully injure destroy or trespass upon or illegally make use of any public property of any kind whatsoever belonging to or in possession of the town trespass for various purposes any person entering upon the lands of another for the purpose of hunting fishing trapping netting gathering fruit wild flowers cultivated flowers shrubbery straw turf vegetables or herbs or cutting timber on such land without the consent of the owner or manager thereof shall be guilty of a misdemeanor and punished in accordance with section 16 of this   no smoking policy in town owned parks or recreation facilities a it shall be unlawful for any person to smoke within any town owned park or recreation facility b smoking shall only be permitted in paved parking lots of such town owned park or recreation facility c violation of such policy shall result in a fine of not less than $1000 nor more than $2500 d each day of a continuing violation of this policy shall be considered a separate and distinct offense  police department composition the police department shall consist of one chief and such other personnel as from time to time may be deemed necessary for the safety and good order of the town appointments a chief the chief of police shall be appointed by the mayor and town council and shall serve as the chief executive of the police force b other police officers the other police officers of the department shall be appointed by the chief of police with approval of the town administrator compensation the compensation for the services of each police department employee shall be set in accordance with the towns compensation plan within the limitations of the annual appropriations for the police department removal or suspension all police department employees are subject to removal or suspension in accordance with the towns personnel policy and procedures manual uniforms the officers of the police department shall be uniformed and equipped as may be designated by the council from time to time all property issued to an officer shall remain the property of the town and shall be returned to the town whenever it is requested by the police chief or the town council police chiefduties and responsibilities a the chief of police shall be responsible to the town administrator and the town council for the execution of the police mission b the chief shall be responsible for the organization efficiency training discipline and morale of the police department c the chief shall ascertain that the operation of the police department and any special units under the chiefs control mutually support one another in all matters requiring support and that a high degree of lateral cooperation and exchange of information is maintained d the chief shall ensure that all books and records are kept in accordance with current applicable federal state and municipal laws as required for the proper performance of the police department police officersduties it shall be the duty of each police officer to arrest andor report any person for violating in any manner the laws or ordinances of the town and failure or neglect to do so shall make such officer liable to suspension or discharge general demeanor each member of the police department at all time shall conduct themselves in a quiet and orderly manner and with a deliberate and efficient determination of enforcing the laws and ordinances of the town offduty conduct each police officer while offduty shall conduct himself in such a manner as to command the respect of the town the officer shall wear no uniform or part thereof while offduty without the expressed approval of the chief of police streets and sidewalks obstructions it shall be unlawful for any person to place any obstruction on or in any way to obstruct any street alley bridge ditch or public rightofway  provided that this section shall not apply to any employee of the city county or state while such employee is immediately and actively engaged in the maintenance improvement or construction of any street sidewalk or public way in the town  nor to utility companies or others performing work thereon with approval by the town placing dangerous substances on streets sidewalks etc it shall be unlawful for any person to place or cause to be placed on any of the sidewalks streets alleys or other public places in the town any tacks nails glass or other sharp instrument or material by which persons or animals may be injured or bicycles automobiles or other vehicles damaged depositing trash it shall be unlawful for any occupant of any house or any merchant shopkeeper or tradesman in town to sweep or deposit in any street public or private alley or public or private yard any paper trash or rubbish or any kind but the same shall be kept in boxes or appropriate receptacles the boxes or receptacles must be provided with a cover suitable or sufficient to contain the contents display of goods a it shall be unlawful for any person without expressed permission from the town council to erect and maintain any table stand or other structure in any street square or alley or upon any sidewalk of the town for the purpose of exposing any commodity for sale of for any other purposes b no personal vehicle or motor vehicle offered for sale shall be placed or displayed within the street rightsofway within the historic district of the town any such motor vehicle so parked placed or displayed may be towed away or otherwise removed at the direction of any police officer and the owner of the vehicle shall be liable for the cost of towing or other removal and storage if the motor vehicle is not reclaimed then it shall be advertised and sold as in the case of sales of motor vehicles for nonpayment of personal property taxes and the costs of towing or other removal and storage shall be deducted from the proceeds of the sale riding bicycles or skateboards on sidewalks it shall be unlawful for any person to ride a bicycle or skateboard on the sidewalks along market street from third street to front street on the sidewalks along second street from church street to powe street and on the sidewalks on both sides of short market wall street within the town between the hours of  am and  pm monday gates and doors opening onto streets and sidewalks it shall be unlawful for any person to build erect or maintain any gate or door in such manner that the same may be opened out on to any sidewalk or street of the town encroaching fences it shall be unlawful for any person to erect any fence that encroaches upon any street of the town or to build any fences along the line of a street before having the property line of such street located by the appropriate official of the town subdivisions article i  in general short title these regulations shall be known cited and references referred to as the subdivision and development regulations of the town of cheraw policy a it is hereby declared to be the policy of the town of cheraw to consider the subdivision of land and the subsequent development of the subdivided plat as subject to the control of the town council to the official land development plan of the council for the orderly planned efficient and economic development of the town b land to be subdivided shall be of such character that it can be used safely for building purposes without danger to health or peril from fire flood or other menace and land shall not be subdivided until available public facilities and improvements exist and proper provisions have been made to drainage water sewage and capital improvements such as schools parks recreation facilities transportation facilities and improvements c the existing and proposed public improvements shall conform to and be properly related to the proposals shown in the land development plan official map and the capital budget and program of the town and it is intended that these regulations shall supplement and facilitate the enforcement of the provisions and standards contained in building and housing codes zoning ordinances comprehensive plans official maps and land use plans and capital budgets and programs of the town purpose these regulations are adopted for the following purposes 1 to protect and provide for the public health safety and general welfare of the town 2 to guide the future growth and development of the town in accordance with a comprehensive plan 3 to provide for adequate light air and privacy to secure safety from fire flood and other danger and to prevent overcrowding of the land and undue congestion of population 4 to protect the character and the social and economic stability of all parts of the town and to encourage the orderly and beneficial development of all parts of the town 5 to protect and conserve the value of land throughout the town and the value of buildings and improvements upon the land and to minimize the conflicts among the uses of land and buildings 6 to guide public and private property and action in order to provide adequate and efficient transportation water sewage schools parks playgrounds recreation and other public requirements and facilities 7 to provide the most beneficial relationship between the users of land and buildings and the circulation of traffic throughout the town having particular regard to the avoidance of congestion in the streets and in the highways and pedestrian traffic movements appropriate to the various uses of land and buildings and to provide for the proper location and width of streets and building lines 8 to establish reasonable standards of design and procedures for subdivisions and resubdivisions in order to further the orderly layout and use of land  and to insure proper legal descriptions in monumenting of subdivided land 9 to insure that public facilities are available and will have a sufficient capacity to serve the proposed subdivision 10 to prevent the pollution of air streams and ponds  to assure the adequacy of drainage facilities  to safeguard the water tables  and to encourage the wise use and management of natural resources throughout the town in order to preserve the integrity stability and beauty of the community and the value of the land 11 to preserve the natural beauty and topography of the town and to insure appropriate development with regard to these natural features 12 to provide for open spaces most efficient spaces and layout of the land including the use of average density in providing for minimum width in area of lot while preserving the density of land as established in the zoning code in the town definitions for the purposes of these regulations certain terms shall be defined as follows governing body the town council of the town of cheraw official maps or plans any maps or plans officially adopted by the town council as a guide for the development of the town and surrounding area rightofway the property improved or unimproved dedicated to and accepted by a unit of government for street or road purposes for vehicular or pedestrian travel the rightofway line generally separates abutting private property from that reserved for public use subdivider any person firm or corporation who undertakes the subdivision of land as herein defined subdivision 1 the division of a tract or parcel of land into two or more lots building sites or other divisions for the purpose whether immediate or future of sale or building development including all development of land involving a new street or a change in existing streets  including resubdivision  and where appropriate to the context relates to the process of subdividing or to the land or area subdivided the following exceptions should not be included within this definition nor be subject to these regulations  however the planning commission shall be informed and have records of such subdivisions a the combination or recombination of portions of previously platted lots where the total number of lots have not increased and the resultant lots are equal to the standards of the governing authority  b the division of land into parcels of five acres or more where no new street is involved plats of such exception shall be received as information by the building official and the planning commission which shall indicate such fact on the plat 2 plats of such exceptions shall be received as information by the building official and the planning commission which shall indicate such fact on the plat official filing of regulations under the enactment of this chapter by the town a copy of this chapter shall be filed in the office of the clerk of court after that time no subdivision plat for any land within the established subdivision jurisdiction shall be filed with or recorded by the county clerk of court until such plat has been submitted to and approved by the building official and the planning commission according to the procedure set forth in this chapter application of regulations no street or other public way or land shall be accepted or maintained  nor shall any municipal water lines sewerage electricity gas street lighting or similar improvements be extended or connected  nor shall any permits be issued by any department of the municipality for construction of a building or other improvement in any subdivision established hereafter which does not meet the requirements set forth in this chapter land subject to flooding land subject to flooding and land otherwise deemed by the planning commission to be unsuitable for development shall not be platted for such uses as may increase danger to health life or property or aggravate the flood hazard but such land within the plat shall be set aside for such uses as shall not be endangered by periodic or occasional inundation effective date this chapter shall take effect and be in force from and after  article ii  plat requirements and review procedures sketch plans a prior to filing an application for preliminary plat for preliminary plat approval the subdivider or his representative shall submit a project description of the proposed subdivision to the building official this description shall contain general information but must contain name of developer  location of project  number and types of structures to be constructed  date utilities required  and any other pertinent information this project description may be in the form of a letter with accompanying sketches oral requests shall not be substituted for the written description b after reviewing the project description the building official shall respond as to the developments feasibility and availability of utilities if roads are to be constructed which are to ultimately become the property of the town they shall also be addressed at this time the building officials review shall also be presented in the form of a written report preliminary plat required the subdivider shall prepare and submit four copies of the preliminary plat and of any supplemental material required for submission to the building official content of preliminary plat the preliminary plat shall be prepared by a registered surveyor or engineer the plat shall be drawn on a standard sheet of 24inch by 36inch paper and to a scale of one inch equals 100 feet or one inch equals 50 feet and shall contain or be accompanied by the following information 1 general information a names and location of adjoining subdivisions streets and the location and ownership of adjoining unsubdivided property b boundaries of the tract to be subdivided with all bearings and distances indicated c existing zoning classification of the tract if any 2 existing site data a town limits lines  property lines  rightsofway  easements  streets  utility transmission lines  storm sewers ditches and culverts  sanitary sewers  water mains  bridges and buildings b wooded areas marshes watercourses ponds and any other similar conditions affecting the site c contours showing the topography of the site at a vertical interval of five feet or as determined by a certified engineer to adequately determine drainage needs d areas subject to flooding accompanied by high water elevation if available 3 proposed site data a street rightsofway pavement widths grade and street names street profiles and cross sections shall be provided when required by the building official or the planning commission b preliminary plans prepared by an engineer for sanitary sewers storm sewers water electricity and gas lines showing connections to existing systems or proposals for developing new water supplies storm drainage and sewerage disposal systems storm and sanitary sewer profiles cross sections and sizes shall be provided when required by the building official or public utility director c other easements and rightsofway including locations dimensions and purposes d contour changes to be made by grading e lot lines lot dimensions lot and block numbers and minimum building setback lines along street rightsofway and rear and side property lines f parks schools sites and other public areas if any g areas to be used for purposes other than residential and public if any with the purpose location and dimension of each indicated 4 other information a name of subdivision and surveyor or engineer b name and address of owner or owners c date of survey and plat preparation north point and graphic scale d surveyors certification of accuracy certifying that the error of closure is at least 000 e site data total acreage in tract  acreage in public or other land usage  average lot size  total number of lots  linear feet in streets f other supplemental materials  any deed restrictions proposed for the subdivision and any other information considered by either the subdivider or the building official to be pertinent to the review of the preliminary plat action of building official on preliminary plat a review  decision the building official shall review and shall approve approve conditionally or disapprove the preliminary plat within 60 days from the date of its submission by the applicant if no action is taken by the building official at the end of the 60 days after submission the preliminary plat shall be deemed to have been approved b approval if the preliminary plat is found to conform to all of the requirements of this chapter approval shall be given by the building official approval shall be noted on at least two copies of the preliminary plat by the building official and town administrator one copy shall be retained in the records of the building official  another shall be given to the subdivider c disapproval  conditional approval if the preliminary plat is disapproved or approved conditionally reasons for such actions shall be stated in writing and signed by the building official the reasons for disapproval shall refer specifically to those parts of the general plan or ordinance or regulation with which the plat does not conform one copy of the reason shall be retained in the records of the building official and another shall be given to the subdivider on conditional approval the building official may require the subdivider to resubmit the preliminary plat with all recommended changes before approval final plat a copies required the subdivider shall submit four dark line prints of the final plat to the town before receiving final approval from the building official at the same time there shall be submitted one set of the proposed plans and specifications for all improvements and any proposed deed restrictions b subdivisions not requiring platting subdivisions that do not involve construction or opening of new streets water or sewer facilities or improvements to existing streets may be accepted by the building official in the form of a final plat such subdivision shall comply with all requirements of these regulations c time of submission the final plat of the proposed subdivision shall be submitted to the building official for final approval within one year of the date on which the preliminary plat was approved if not submitted for final approval within such time the preliminary plat shall be considered as having been disapproved unless the building official agrees to an extension of time d recording the final plat shall constitute only that portion of the approved preliminary plat which the subdivider proposes to record and develop at the time the final plat shall be filed in the office of the county clerk of court within 30 days after approval of or it not approval shall be considered void e contents the final plat shall conform substantially to the preliminary plat as it was approved the final plat shall be prepared by a registered surveyor or engineer and shall be drawn on a standard sheet of 24inch by 36inch paper to a scale of one inch equals 100 feet or one inch equals 50 feet it shall contain or be accompanied by the following information 1 survey data a exact boundary of the tract to be subdivided  the error of closure shall be at least 000 b names and location of adjoining subdivisions and streets location and ownership of adjoining unsubdivided property c accurate location and description of all monuments markets and control points d sufficient engineering data to determine regularly and reproduce on the ground every straight or curved boundary line street line lot line rightofway line easement line and setback line including linear dimensions bearings or deflection angles tangents radii arcs chords and central angles all dimensions shall be measured to the nearest onehundredth of a foot and all angles to the nearest minute e the error of linear closure for lots shall be at least 000 2 site data a all rightsofway easements and areas to be dedicated to public use with the purpose of each stated b areas to be used for purposes other than residential and public if any with the purpose location and dimensions of each indicated c lot and block numbers  street names d such cross section and profiles of streets as may be required by the building official and public utility director e such plans for water mains sanitary sewers and storm sewers showing sizes cross sections and profiles as required by the building official and the public utility director 3 other information a name of subdivision owner and surveyor or engineer b date of survey and plat preparation  north arrow  graphic scale c deed restrictions proposed for the subdivision if any d any other information considered by either the subdivider or the building official to be pertinent to the review of the final plat f certificates the following signed certificates shall be shown on the original and all copies of the final plat submitted to the building official 1 certificate of ownership and dedication 2 certificate of approval of water supply and sewage disposal systems where necessary 3 certificates of surveying and mapping g signed statement a statement signed by the town administrator as to the towns acceptance of utilities action of building official on final plat a approval the building official shall approve or disapprove the final plat within 60 days after it has been submitted for final approval approval and the date thereof shall be known on the plat over the signature of the building official and town administrator if no action is taken by the building official at the end of the 60 days after submission the plat shall be deemed to have been approved b disapproval if the final plat is disapproved by the building official the grounds for such action shall be stated in writing the reasons for disapproval shall refer specifically to those parts of the general plan or ordinance or regulation with which the plat does not conform one copy of the reasons for disapproval shall be retained in the records of the building official and another shall be given to the subdivider c reconciliation with preliminary plat during review of the final plat the building official shall check the final plat against the preliminary plat the building official shall appoint an engineer or surveyor to check the accuracy of the subdivision layout and the final plat if substantial errors are found the cost of checking the plat shall be charged to the developer d conformity to land development plan all proposed subdivisions of land shall conform to the applicable portions of the land development plan for the town e post approval procedure after final approval the subdivider shall file the original approved final plat with certificates with the county clerk of court the subdivider shall provide the building official with one dark line print thereof article iii  design standards minimum requirements the following design standards shall be considered minimum requirements  however higher standards are to be encouraged in subdivision designs if only minimum standards are used the result will be a standardized and monotonous urban area subdivision designs should carry out the purpose of the general plan in this chapter but not be limited to the minimum requirements as provided in this article easements a easements not less than 20 feet wide centered on side or rear lot lines shall be provided where necessary for use by public or private utilities where a subdivision is traversed by a water course drainage way channel or stream they shall be provided a storm water easement or drainage rightofway conforming substantially with the lines of such water course and of sufficient width to carry off storm water b the governing body concerned shall maintain only those easements it accepts for public maintenance as will be adequate for this purpose parallel streets or parkways may be required in connection therewith blocks a lengths 1 the lengths widths and shapes of blocks shall be determined with regard for the following a provision of adequate building sites suitable to the special needs for the types of use contemplated b zoning requirements as to lot sizes and dimensions c needs for convenient access circulation control and safety of street traffic d limitations and opportunities of topography 2 blocks for residential use shall be not longer than 2400 feet and shall not be less than 200 feet in length measured along the center line of the block or as directed by the building official b width blocks used for residential purposes should be of sufficient width to allow for two tiers of lots and appropriate depth where practical considering natural topography or manmade boundaries blocks intended for business and industrial use shall be of a width suitable for the intended use with due allowance for offstreet parking and loading facilities size width depth shape and orientation shall be appropriate for the location of the subdivision and for the type of development and use contemplated all lots shall conform to the requirements of the zoning chapter  of this   building lines in all residential subdivisions the minimum setback from the street rightofway or property line shall be in conformance with the applicable zoning classifications public sites and open spaces where a proposed park playground school or other public use shown in the general plan is located in whole or in part of a subdivision the building official may require the reservation of such area for a period not exceeding 90 days from the date of approval of the preliminary plat in order to give the public body concerned opportunity to acquire such site for that expressed purpose areas subject to flooding a plat of a proposed subdivision submitted to the building official and public utility director for approval which contains land subject to flooding shall have such areas delineated as being subject to flooding no new construction shall take place within 50 feet of a natural drainage way or any area so designated as a flood prone area by the federal emergency management agency article iv  improvements water lines  fire hydrants every lot in every subdivision shall be provided with an approved water supply it shall have an adequate supply of water for domestic and fire purposes with sufficient pressure in the main to meet the minimum standards for fire purposes at all times in accordance with underwriters standards the water mains in the subdivision shall 1 be of sufficient size to provide at least one standard fire hydrant within 1000 feet to be measured along rightsofway of streets or public ways of each residence or other structures and 500 feet of any commercial or industrial buildings and at locations designated by the fire chief 2 provide circulation within the system where practical 3 should the town require a larger water line to be installed in order to allow for future growth the town will be responsible for the cost between the larger size line and that required for development 4 comply will all rules and standards of the water and fire departments of the town a where a public water main in the opinion of the building official and public utility director is reasonably accessible the subdivider shall connect with such water main and provide a connection stubout for each lot for the purpose of this section reasonably accessible is considered 1000 feet from the property proposed to be subdivided b the developer shall be required to furnish the following documents to the town upon the installation of such water lines 1 certificate of approval from dhec for use of water system 2 asbuilt drawings of all work completed 3 a oneyear warranty on all lines installed by the developer sanitary sewer system a where a public sanitary sewer is reasonably accessible the subdivider shall connect with such sanitary sewer and provide a connection with cleanout for each lot for the purpose of this section reasonably accessible is considered 1000 feet from the property proposed to be subdivided the design grade and capacity shall be approved by the public utility director  however in no event shall the town be required to furnish sewer service to persons or subdivisions outside the corporate limits of the town b the developer shall be required to furnish the following documents to the town upon the installation of such water lines 1 certificate of approval and acceptance by dhec 2 asbuilt drawings of all work completed 3 a oneyear warranty on all lines installed by the developer sanitary sewer lines the subdivider shall install sanitary sewers that are large enough to provide adequate service to every house in the subdivision when it is completely developed sanitary sewers shall be installed in accordance with town specifications and standards should the town require a larger sewer line to be installed in order to allow for future growth the town will be responsible for the cost between the larger size line and that required for the development storm sewers and drainage an adequate storm drainage system designed to protect the proposed development from flooding shall be installed in accordance with good engineering practices the system shall be adequate to carry all storm water in its drainage area and shall complement systems on adjacent property upstream and downstream where a public storm sewer is reasonably accessible as determined by the building official and the public works director the subdivider shall connect with such drainage system the developer shall also be required to submit to the town an easement for any drainage ditch draining more than one lot the size of such easement shall be determined by the public works director streets a streets to be developed developers shall be required to develop paved streets in any development in accordance with acceptable standards b system design and improvements the street system shall be designed to permit the safe efficient and orderly movement of traffic  to have a simple and logical pattern  to respect natural features and topography  and to present an attractive streetscape 1 layout and alignment a proposed streets shall be coordinated with the street system in the surrounding area and where possible shall provide for the continuation of existing streets abutting the development b all streets shall be opened to the exterior property lines of the development unless permanently terminated by a vehicular turnaround or an intersection with another street c no half street shall be permitted 2 alleys a alleys are not permitted in residential subdivisions b paved alleys are permitted in commercial and industrial developments to provide service access offstreet loading and unloading and parking consistent with and adequate for the uses proposed 3 culsdesac a deadend streets designed to be permanently closed at one end shall not exceed 1000 feet in length measured from the rightofway of the intersecting street to the center point of the turnaround b turnarounds shall be provided at the closed end of the street 4 intersections a no more than two streets shall intersect at any one point b all streets shall intersect as nearly as possible at 90degree angles c streets entering upon opposite sides of a given street shall have their center lines directly opposite or shall be offset a minimum distance of 150 feet for minor streets and 400 feet for major streets measured along the center line of the streets being intersected d street intersections shall be located at least 150 feet from the rightofway of any railroad track measured from the center point of the intersection to the railroad rightofway nearest the intersection e private drives shall not intersect a public street within 40 feet of an intersection measured from the street rightofway 5 rightofway lane and pavement widths minimum street rightofway lane and pavement widths shall be as follows classification pavement width rightofway width minor street 50 feet  with barrier curb 25 feet 50 feet  with roll curb 25 feet 50 feet  with valley gutter 50 feet major street 66 feet  with barrier curb 27 feet 66 feet  with roll curb 36 feet 66 feet  with valley gutter 36 feet 66 feet alley 18 feet 22 feet driveway tiles the property owner shall be responsible for the placement of proper driveway drainage tiles as each lot is developed or until such time that the county or the state department of transportation assumes such responsibility survey accuracy the error of lineage closure for land surveys shall not exceed one foot per 10000 feet of perimeter of land 000 article v  town participation in installation of water and sewer mains policy the town may participate in the installation of water mains and sanitary sewer lines in any new and undeveloped subdivision for the sale of lots within the corporate limits of the town as provided in this article town participation the owner or owners of any such subdivision within the town limits after approval of subdivision plat by the building official and with the consent permission and approval of the town council shall install water mains and sanitary sewer lines at their own expense in such subdivisions the town requires that all improvements made in the public rightsofway and easements of the subdivision be supervised by an approved licensed engineer whose services would be retained by the developer if and when the water mains and sanitary sewer lines are approved and accepted by the town as part of the water works and sanitary sewer systems of the town then the town shall reimburse the developer at a rate as herein described method of reimbursement a reimbursement to the developer of such water mains and sanitary sewer lines shall be contingent upon storm sewers having been installed by the developer when required in accordance with the approved plat b a developer shall be eligible for reimbursement from the town for the installation of water mains and sanitary sewer lines as each individual lot within the subdivision has upon it a completely constructed house which is connected to the towns utilities  that is reimbursement shall be made to the developer on a lot by lot basis the rate of reimbursement to the developer shall be $1000 per front foot with a minimum of no less than $75000 and a maximum not to exceed $150000 per lot c any commercial industrial or multiplefamily housing projects will be dealt with on a casebycase basis term of agreement a this agreement for reimbursement will terminate ten years after the date of the approval of the agreement by the town council b this reimbursement amount shall be reviewed by council from time to time and revised as seen fit to maintain a fair and equitable return to the developer article vi  administration and enforcement effect of plat approval on dedication the approval of a plat by the building official and the planning commission shall not be deemed to constitute or affect an acceptance by the governing body of the dedication of any street or other ground shown upon the plat variances whenever the tract to be divided is of such unusual size or shape or is surrounded by such development or unusual conditions that strict application of the requirements in this chapter would result in substantial hardship or inequity the planning commission may vary or modify except as otherwise indicated requirements of design but not of procedure or improvements so that the subdivider may develop the property in a reasonable manner but so at the same time the public welfare is protected and the general intent and spirit of this chapter is preserved amendments this chapter may be amended form time to time by the town council  however no amendment shall become effective unless it shall have been submitted to the planning commission for review and recommendations the planning commission shall have 60 days within which to submit its report to the town council if the planning commission fails to submit a report within the specified time period it shall be deemed to have approved the proposed amendment enforcement a no plat of any subdivision shall be entitled to be recorded in the office of the clerk of court of chesterfield county or shall have any validity until it has been approved in the manner prescribed herein b it shall be unlawful for the owner or the agent of any owner to transfer or sell any land by reference to or by other use of a plat unless such plat has been approved as prescribed herein the town council may enjoin such transfer sale or agreement by appropriate legal action c in case of any violation of this chapter the town administrator or any appropriate official as may be designated by the planning commission is authorized and directed to institute legal action to put an end to such violations interpretation and conflict in interpreting and applying the provisions of this chapter the provisions shall be held to be minimum requirements necessary to uphold the purpose of this chapter it is not intended by this chapter to interfere with or abrogate or annul and easements covenants or other agreements between parties provided however where this chapter imposes greater restrictions on the subdivision andor use of buildings or land or requires more open spaces or more stringent development standards than required by other resolutions ordinances rules or regulations or by easements covenants or agreements the provisions of this chapter shall govern when the provisions of any other statute require more restrictive standards than are required by the regulations of this chapter the provisions of each statute shall govern sale of plat before approval  remedy a after the adoption of this chapter any person who being the owner or agent of the owner of any land located within the established subdivision jurisdiction transfers or sells or agrees to sell or negotiates to sell any land by reference to or exhibition of or by other use of a plat of a subdivision before such plat has been approved by the building official and the planning commission and recorded in the office of the county clerk of court shall forfeit and pay a penalty of $25000 to the town for each lot or parcel so transferred or sold or deeded or negotiated to be sold b the description of such lot or parcel by metes and bounds in the instrument of transfer or other document used in the process of selling or transferring such lot or parcel shall not exempt the transaction from such penalties or from the remedy provided in this section the town attorney or other official designated by the town may enjoin such transfer or sale or agreement by an action for injunction brought in any court of competent jurisdiction and may also recover such penalty by civil action in any court of competent jurisdiction penalty any violation of this chapter will be punishable by a fine not exceeding $50000 or imprisonment not exceeding 30 days in accordance with sc laws  5730 as amended taxation article i  in general adoption of budget the cheraw town council shall prepare a budget for the fiscal year ending june of each year and estimated revenues for payment of same the budget shall be made a part hereof by reference as fully as if incorporated herein administration of budget the town administrator shall administer the budget and shall authorize the transfer of appropriated funds within and between departments as necessary to achieve the goals of the annual budget taxes imposed a tax to cover the fiscal year period from july 1 to june 30 of the following year shall be established annually by the town council said tax rates shall be levied on the assessed value of real estate and personal property of every description known and used by the town of cheraw except such as exempt from the taxation under the constitution and laws of the state of south carolina assessments prepared by county the town shall utilize the tax assessment of evaluation of properties prepared by the county auditor and county tax assessor as the basis for determining the assessments of taxes for municipal purposes billing dates  penalties a the billing dates the dates and amount of penalty which shall be levied for delinquent taxes shall be as follows tax notices for each calendar year shall be mailed in october and are payable by january 15 of the following year b penalty dates for payments paid in the following calendar year are subject to a penalty of three percent on or after january 16 ten percent if paid by february 1 and 15 percent plus collection costs if paid by march 16 after june 1 additional collection costs will be added tax collector  delinquent tax sale the chesterfield county treasurer shall serve as the collection agency for the real estate taxes for the town and shall remit said portion to the town according to a prescribed schedule in a timely manner chesterfield county shall also handle the sale of all delinquent sales for the town exemption of certain manufacturing establishments from ad valorem taxation a there shall be exempt from ad valorem taxation within the town of cheraw all new manufacturing establishments located wholly within the corporate limits of the town of cheraw for two years from the establishment and all additions to the existing manufacturing establishments located wholly within the town for two years from the time each such addition is made if the costs of such addition is $5000000 or more provided however that the exemption shall first apply to qualified properties upon which a tax would ordinarily be paid beginning  such additions shall include additional machinery and equipment installed in the manufacturing establishment b no new manufacturing establishment shall be entitled to the exemption unless construction of the new manufacturing establishment is commenced after  c no additions to existing manufacturing establishments shall be entitled to the exemption unless construction of the new addition is commenced after  d exemptions granted pursuant to this section shall not result in any refund of taxes e any manufacturing establishment seeking to obtain the exemption from ad valorem taxes levied by the town of cheraw shall comply with all requirements of state law to obtain exemption of local property taxes on manufacturing property allowed under sc laws 197  13372207 as amended f except with respect to the question of whether or not the property was constructed or acquired after the effective date of this section the town clerk shall annually use information provided by the south carolina department of revenue to the appropriate county official under sc laws 197  123145 as amended g the tax exempt status shall be revoked if it is determined that the property does not qualify annually under the provisions of the constitution the general laws of this state and this section h if it is found within three years from the date that taxes would have been due on property that has been granted an exemption that the exemption was improperly granted the town clerk upon receiving notice thereof shall enter on the duplicate the taxes that would have been due for any years that the property escaped taxation with a ten percent penalty added thereto i the annexation of existing manufacturing establishments into the town of cheraw shall not result in the creation of a new manufacturing establishment which would be entitled to an exemption under this section article ii  local hospitality fee declaration of policy  purpose  intent this article is enacted to preserve the general health safety and welfare of the general public and to promote and enhance the tourism industry in the cheraw area by imposing a fee for the purpose of creating a fund which will be utilized for purposes enumerated in sc laws  61730a as such may be amended local hospitality fee of two percent there is hereby imposed a local hospitality fee of two percent on the gross proceeds of the sale of all prepared meals and beverages served by any establishment within the town of cheraw including those licensed for onpremise consumption of alcoholic beverages beer or wine within the town payment of fee a payment of the fee established herein shall be the liability of the consumer of the services for items described in section 179 the fee shall be paid at the time of delivery of the services or items to which the fee applies and shall be collected by the provider or seller of the items b the fee collected by the seller or provider of services or items as required under section 179 shall be remitted to the town as follows 1 on a monthly basis when the estimated amount of average collections is more than $5000 a month 2 on a quarterly basis when the estimated amount of average collections is between $2500 a month to $5000 a month 3 on an annual basis when the amount of average collections is less than $2500 a month c total collections and required reports shall be submitted to the town by the twentieth day of the month and shall cover sales for the pervious previous month d a copy of the completed south carolina state sales and use return form form st3 shall be attached along with such required forms prepared by the town when a hospitality fee return is filed and the fees due are paid in full on or before the final due date the filer is allowed a discount of two percent on the fees shown to be due by the return payments covered under the provisions of subsection 1710b2 shall be submitted quarterly by the twentieth day of january april july and october for the previous quarterly sales or annually by the twentieth of january for the calendar year sales as provided in subsection 1710b3 when the twentieth of the month falls on a weekend or a holiday the town will accept without penalty payment on the following work day e any collections not remitted by the deadlines outlined in this article shall be subject to a penalty of five percent of the unpaid amount for any calendar month or portion thereof after the due date until paid the failure to collect from patrons the amount imposed by this article shall not relieve any establishment subject to this article form making the required remittance f any person violating this article shall be deemed guilty of an offense and shall be subject to punishment by a fine of not more than $50000 or imprisonment for up to 30 days or both each day of violation shall be considered a separate offense punishment for violation shall not relieve the offender of liability for delinquent amount penalties and costs provided for herein local hospitality fee fund established a separate fund or account to be known as the local hospitality fee account shall be established and all revenues received from the hospitality fee shall be deposited into this account and shall remain segregated from the general fund the principal and any interest accrued from this account shall be expended only as permitted in section 1712 permitted use of funds the town is hereby authorized to utilize funds collected from the imposition of the hospitality fee for the purposes enumerated in sc laws  61730 as such may be amended inspection and audits for the purposes of enforcing the provisions of this section the town clerk licensing and permitting official or any other authorized agent of the town is empowered to enter upon the premises of any person subject to this section to make inspection examine andor audit the books and records and it shall be unlawful for any person to fail or refuse to make available the necessary books and records in the event that the audit or inspection reveals that the establishment has filed false information the cost of the audit shall be added to the corrected amount due and late penalties in addition to other penalties provided herein each day of failure to pay the proper fee shall constitute a separate offense the town clerk licensing and permitting official or other authorized agent of the town shall make systematic inspections of the businesses within the town to ensure compliance with this section records of inspections and audits shall not be deemed public records and shall not be released by the town authorization for use authorization to utilize revenues from the local hospitality fee account shall be by the annual budget ordinance or budget amendment duly adopted by the town council severability if any section phrase sentence or portion of this article is for any reason held invalid or unconstitutional by any court of competent jurisdiction such section phrase sentence or portion shall be deemed a separate distinct and independent provision and such holding shall not affect of the remaining sections phrases sentences or portions thereof this article shall become effective immediately upon its adopting and all applicable businesses shall be responsible for collecting and remitting the tax beginning on  article iii  local accommodations tax imposition there is hereby imposed a local accommodations tax of three percent upon the gross proceeds derived from rental or charges for accommodations furnished to transients as is more fully defined and described in sc laws 197  61520 as amended payment of tax  past due penalty payment of the accommodations tax as herein established shall be remitted to the town on a monthly basis along with such return forms as established by the town for such purposes not later than the twentieth day of the month and shall the tax due for the previous month any tax not timely remitted shall be subject to a penalty of five percent of the sum owed for each month or portion thereof until paid use of revenue the revenue generated by the local accommodations tax with accumulated interest placed in the local accommodations tax fund shall be used exclusively for the following purposes 1 tourismrelated buildings including but not limited to civic enters coliseums and aquariums  2 cultural recreational or historic facilities  3 beach access and renourishment  4 highways roads streets and bridges providing access to tourist destinations  5 advertisements and promotions related to tourism development  or 6 water and sewer infrastructure to serve tourismrelated demand taxicabs definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this article shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning taxicab means any motor vehicle used for or engaged in the transportation of passengers for hire or compensation except vehicles commonly known as buses compliance  exceptions no person shall drive a taxicab or engage in the business of operating taxicabs upon the town streets until that person has complied with this article this article shall not apply to vehicles operating under a special franchise or to vehicles transporting persons to or from school or college ownership of vehicle required it shall be unlawful for any person to engage in the business of operating or maintaining taxicabs in the town pursuant to a license issued in accordance with this section unless such person shall be the bona fide owner of the motor vehicles so operated or maintained all such persons shall deposit with the town a copy of certificate or other satisfactory evidence covering each vehicle so operated or maintained lease of vehicles to third parties it shall be unlawful for any person to engage in the business of operating or maintaining taxicabs in the town pursuant to a license issued in accordance with this section to rent or lease any motor vehicle the operation of which is covered under such license to any other person without first surrendering to the town for cancellation the license covering the operation of such motor vehicle as a taxicab application for operators business license  contents a any person desiring a license to operate a taxicab business shall file any application for a license upon a form furnished by the town provided that the license shall be issued within 30 days after a written application has been made b the application referred to in subsection a shall give the full name age and home address of the applicant and shall state whether or not he has been convicted of a violation of any town ordinance or of any state or federal law and if so the number of times the dates and the nature of the violations and all other information that shall be required c if the applicant for a license to operate a taxicab business is a firm or corporation the requirements of subsections a and b of this section shall be complied with by each member of the firm or by the principal or managing officer of the corporation in charge of actual operation of the business in the town age limit of licensees  residency requirement a no license for the operation of a taxicab business or a taxicab drivers permit shall be issued to any person under the age of 21 years b no license for the operation of a taxicab business shall be issued to any person who has not for a period of six months immediately prior to the date of the application therefore resided in the county taxicab license fee the taxicab business must pay a business license fee for the operation of the business plus an additional fee of $2500 per year per taxicab limitation on the number of taxicabs the number of licensed taxicabs for any one business is limited to 12 liability insurance requirement no license shall be issued by the town to any person to operate a taxicab or other like vehicle within the town unless the vehicle is covered by a paidinfull annual liability insurance policy with limits of at least $10000000 per individual  $20000000 per incident  and $2500000 for property damage proof of such annual paidinfull insurance coverage must be exhibited to the town by delivering a copy of the liability insurance policy for each vehicle insured and a paid receipt for the premium indicating that the annual insurance coverage is paidinfull notice of cancellation of insurance each policy of insurance required under this section shall contain a clause authorizing and directing the insurer to notify the town of any cancellation thereof and immediately upon notice of cancellation the town shall revoke the license to operate a taxicab or other like vehicle within the town issuance of license a the town clerk shall collect correlate and submit to the town council the application and all other reports of information and findings required under this section together with a report of any additional pertinent information and a recommendation b the town council shall review the application finding and report and recommendations and shall authorize the issuance of a license to operate a taxicab business if it finds that the applicant therefore has complied with all requirements of this section and is fit willing and able to perform public transportation and to conform to this chapter and that further taxicab service in the town is required by public convenience and necessity in making these findings the town council shall take into consideration the number of taxicabs already in operation whether existing transportation is adequate to meet the public need the probable effect of increased service on local traffic conditions and the character experience and responsibility of the applicant c upon authorization by the town council the town clerk shall issue to the applicant a license to operate a taxicab business upon payment to the town of the license fee required identification markings upon the issuance of any license for the operation of a taxicab business the licensee shall paint or affix to each side and the rear of each vehicle operated under his license in letters at least two inches high the number of the license and the name of the holder thereof or in the alternative he shall place on the top near the front a sign which may be illuminated designating the vehicle as a taxicab and giving the license number magnetic signs may be substituted for the required signs report of suspicious persons every taxicab driver shall report to the police department any suspicious person or activity coming to his attention as soon as possible or immediately upon the discharge of any such person from his vehicle vehicles from other areas taxicabs or other public vehicles for hire having no town license and whose place of business is not in the town may bring passengers into town but shall not solicit any passengers for any destination within or outside the town limits employment of driver without taxicab drivers permit prohibited it shall be unlawful for any person engaged in the business of operating or maintaining taxicabs pursuant to this section to permit the driving of such taxicab in the town by any person to whom a taxicab drivers permit shall not have been granted and currently in effect revocation of taxicab drivers permit a taxicab drivers permits shall be revoked upon bond forfeiture guilty plea or conviction in connection with the violation of any town ordinance or state statute relating to the operation of motor vehicles appeals upon the failure of the town to issue a taxicab drivers permit or upon the towns revocation of a taxicab drivers permit such aggrieved applicant or licensee shall have the right to appeal to the town council and be heard in connection therewith water and sewer article i  waterworks liability of owner for broken meters a the individual contracting for water service with the town of cheraw shall be responsible for any negligent or willful damage to meters meter boxes valves locking devices or other fixtures pertaining to water service and the actual cost of labor and materials used in replacement or repair of such damaged fixtures shall be added to the customers utility bill b it shall be unlawful for any person to receive water from any part of the towns water system without a valid permitapproval from the town clerk or without an inservice meter it shall be unlawful for any person to tamper with open close remove bypass or otherwise deal with any fire hydrant valve valve box meter meter box tank pump structure or fixture appertaining to the towns water system upon conviction there shall be a fine imposed of not less than $20000 for the first offense each subsequent offense shall upon conviction be imposed a fee of an additional $10000 with a maximum fine not to exceed $50000 or imprisonment for a period not exceeding 30 days
