provisions have been included as  191 see also the table when connection and meter required a every residence or other building which is located within 250 feet of any water main or within 250 feet of any sewer collector line shall be connected thereto and shall utilize the same for water and for the disposal of all sewage originating on said premises such connections shall be forthwith made and for the purposes of the penal provisions of this chapter subsection 191b each day during which such building shall not be connected to such water main or collector line shall be a separate offense and punishable as hereinafter provided b all water service shall be rendered upon a meter basis reading of meters  billing  second notices  discontinuation of service and reconnection fee a all meters shall be read once a month and water bills shall be due when rendered and payable in their entirety within 30 days customers will receive a second notice concerning their account approximately seven days prior to their service being terminated b if any bill remains unpaid at the end of the 30day period thereafter all service to such user shall be discontinued usually around the sixteenth of the month until such user shall have paid the current bill and penalties together with a reconnection fee of $1500 water bill adjustment policy a water users experiencing a severe increase in their utility bill may be eligible for an adjustment to that bill if and only if the bill being considered is twice the normal sixmonth average for water and sewer charges for that individual account b no adjustments will be made to any bill within the first six months of activity c the garbage fee meter rent and service fee will not be included in determining the sixmonth average for ones account d water users may have no more than two adjustments to their account during any calendar year e a leak will be defined as the loss of water due to broken or burst water linespipes an improperly functioning toilet or a damaged value valve on a water heater outside spigots left on will not be considered a leak and therefore no adjustment will be made on that individuals account f individuals requesting such adjustments must have had a valid leak and show some proof of repair g the formula for determining the adjustment to the customers water and sewer bill will be as follows the high bill minus the sixmonth average equals the base rate the base rate divided by two equals the charges the charges plus the sixmonth average equals the total adjusted water and sewer bill after the adjustment to the water and sewer bill the garbage meter rent and service fee will be added for a final adjusted bill connection fees for each new residential and commercial connection to the towns water system the person or firm applying for such service shall pay connection fees in the following amounts for each new residential and commercial connection to the towns water system the person or firm applying for such service shall pay connection fees in the following amounts a for standard water connections water meter size inside town outside town 34 $60000 $80000 1 $70000 $110000 112 $110000 $192500 2 $160000 $292500 b all water connections over two inches for intown customers are charged at a rate equal to the towns actual cost of installation plus 20 percent with a minimum charge of $350000 outoftown customers will be charged at a rate equal to the towns actual cost of installation plus 40 percent with a minimum charge of $650000 c a backflow prevention device may be required for any residence business or industry frequent testing of this device will be required of every business at regular intervals d water connection to apartment units or multibusiness commercial complexes shall be determined in one of two ways 1 if the town installs the water line to the property line the fee will be based on the cost of providing such service plus 20 percent 40 percent for outoftown customers plus an additional fee equal to the tap fee for each unit  or 2 if the developer installs the water line and all appurtenances to meet the towns specifications the developer will only pay $7500 per unit as a connection fee if the property is intown and $20000 per unit if the property is outoftown e no individual will be allowed to connect to any tap which has been inactive for a period of five years without first paying a new connection fee f there shall be no refund for unused or abandoned taps g connections for meters larger than two inches if installed to the towns specifications by the owners contractor shall be charged $60000 per connection for customers inside town and $110000 per connection for customers outoftown ownership of these meters shall be with the customer who shall be responsible for meter testing at intervals not exceeding five years and any necessary repairs in accordance with a fiveyear schedule or as necessitated by performance logarithm base 10 of the reciprocal of the weight of hydrogen ions in grams per liter of solution a ph of 70 is considered neutral a stabilized ph will be considered a ph which does not change beyond the specified limits when the waste is subjected to aeration a ph below 70 is acid and above is alkaline ppm parts per million by weight expressed by pounds one million pounds of water or sewage equals approximately 120000 gallons eight and thirtyfour onehundredths 834 pounds in one million gallons of water equals one ppm pretreatment the reduction of the amount of pollutants the elimination of pollutants or the alteration of the nature of pollutant properties in wastewater prior to or in lieu of discharging or otherwise introducing such pollutants into a potw process wastewater any water which during manufacturing or processing comes into direct contact with or results from the production of or use of any raw material intermediate product finished product byproduct or waste product excluded are sanitary noncontact cooling water and boiler wastewaters properly shredded garbage the wastes from the preparation cooking and dispensing of food that has been shredded to such degree that all particles will be carried freely under the flow conditions normally prevailing in public sewers with no particles greater than 12inch in any dimension public sewer a sewer in which all owners of abutting properties shall have equal rights and is controlled by public authority publicly owned treatment works potw the treatment works which are owned by the town of cheraw this includes any devices and systems used in the storage treatment recycling and reclamation of municipal sewage or industrial wastes of a liquid nature it also includes sewers pipes and other conveyances only if they convey wastewater to a potw treatment plant receiving stream that body of water stream or watercourse receiving the discharge waters from the sewage treatment plant or formed by the discharge of the sewage treatment plant sanitary sewer a sewer which carries sewage or polluted industrial wastes and to which storm surface and ground waters or unpolluted industrial wastes are not intentionally admitted sewage a combination of the watercarried wastes from residences businesses institutions and industrial establishments sewerage works all facilities for collecting pumping treating and disposing of sewage sewer a pipe or conduit for carrying sewage sewage treatment plant any arrangement or device and structures for treating sewage shall may shall is mandatory  may is permissive significant industrial user siu all industrial users subject to categorical pretreatment standards under 40 cfr 4036 and 40 cfr subchapter n  and any other industrial user that discharges an average of 25000 gallons per day or more of process wastewater to the potw excluding sanitary noncontact cooling and boiler blowdown wastewater  contributes a process wastestream which makes up five percent or more of the average dry weather hydraulic or organic capacity of the potw  or is designated as such by the approving authority on the basis that the industrial user has a reasonable potential for adversely affecting the potws operation or for violating any pretreatment standard or requirement significant noncompliance snc shall be as follows 1 chronic violations sixtysix percent or more of all measurements taken during a sixmonth period exceed by any magnitude the daily maximum limit or the average limit for the same pollutant parameter 2 technical review criteria trc violations thirtythree percent or more of all the measurements taken during a sixmonth period for the same parameter equal or exceed the product of the daily maximum limit multiplied by the applicable trc for conventional pollutants bod tss and fats oil and grease trc   14 or 40% over the limit for all other pollutants except ph trc   12 or 20% over the limit 3 any other violation of a pretreatment effluent limit daily maximum or monthly average that the approving authority determines has caused alone or in combination with other discharges interference or pass including endangering the health of the treatment system personnel or the general public 4 any discharge causing imminent endangerment to human healthwelfare or to the environment and resulting in the potws use of its emergency authority to halt or prevent such a discharge 5 failure to meet within 90 days after the scheduled date a compliance schedule milestone contained in a wastewater discharge permit or enforcement order for starting construction completing construction or attaining final compliance 6 failure to provide within 30 days after the due date required compliance reports periodic selfmonitoring reports and reports on compliance with compliance schedules 7 failure to accurately report noncompliance 8 any other violation or group of violations which the approving authority determines will adversely affect the operation or implementation of the local pretreatment program storm sewer or storm drain a sewer which carries storm and surface waters and drainage but excludes sewage or polluted industrial wastes suspended solids solids that either float on the surface of or are in suspension in water sewage or other liquids  and which are removable by laboratory filters town the town of cheraw south carolina or any duly authorized officials acting in its behalf upset an exceptional incident in which there is unintentional and temporarily noncompliance with pretreatment standards because of factors beyond the reasonable control of the industrial user an upset does not include noncompliance to the extent caused by operational error improperly designed treatment facilities inadequate treatment facilities lack of preventive maintenance or careless or improper operations amendments the town duly qualified officers reserves the right to amend this article in part or in whole whenever it may deem necessary but such right will be exercised only after due notice by publication one time in the daily press 90 days before any final action protection of system against damage no person shall maliciously willfully or negligently break damage destroy uncover deface or tamper with any equipment or materials belonging to the town of cheraw and used for this purpose of making measurements tests or examinations and left upon the premises of a person discharging wastes into the sewer this protection against damage shall also apply to any part of the public sewer system any person violating this provision shall be subject to immediate arrest and prosecution division 2  discharge regulations prohibited discharges to public sanitary sewers except as hereinafter provided no person shall discharge or cause to be discharged any of the following described water or wastes to any public sanitary sewer 1 any clothing rags textile remnants or wastes cloth scraps etc except fibers scraps etc which will not pass onequarterinch mesh screen or its equivalent 2 any liquid or vapor having a temperature higher than 160 degrees fahrenheit 3 any water or waste containing more than 100 parts per million by weight of fats oil or grease 4 any liquids solids or gases which by reason of their nature or quality create a fire or explosion hazard in the potw including but not limited to wastestreams with a closed cup flashpoint of less than 140 degrees fahrenheit using the test methods specified in 40 cfr 2612 or be in any way injurious to persons or damaging to the sewage system the sewage treatment works or the operation of the sewage treatment works 5 any liquid wastes in which the suspended solids exceed 600 parts per million by weight 6 any liquid wastes having bod of more than 600 parts per million except as hereinafter provided for 7 any waters or wastes having a stabilized ph lower that 50 or higher than 110 or having other corrosive property capable of causing damage or hazard to structures equipment or personnel of the sewage works 8 any waters or wastes containing a poisonous or toxic substance or other materials in sufficient quantity to injure or interfere with any sewage treatment process or constitute a hazard to humans or animals or create any hazard in the receiving stream at the sewage treatment plant 9 any noxious or malodorous gas or substance capable of creating a public nuisance 10 any garbage that has not been properly shredded 11 any ashes cinders sand mud straw shavings metal glass bones feathers tar plastics wood paunch manure butchers offal or any or solid or viscous substances capable of causing obstruction to the flow in sewers or other interference with the proper operation of the sewage collection system or the sewage treatment works 12 any materials which form excessive amounts of scum that may interfere with the operation of the sewage treatment works or cause undue additional labor in connection with its operation 13 any waters or wastes containing dyes or other color which cannot be removed by biological processes and which require special chemical treatment 14 any waters or wastes containing lint in such quantities as to be detrimental to sewer lines sewage pumps or sewage treatment works 15 any substance which may cause the sewage treatment works effluent or other product such as residues sludges or scums to be unsuitable for reclamation reuse or disposal 16 any substance which may cause interference with the potw 17 any trucked or hauled pollutant except at discharge points designated by the potw additional prohibited discharges no person shall discharge or cause to be discharged into any sanitary sewers any stormwater surface water uncontaminated groundwater roof runoff subsurface drainage uncontaminated noncontact cooling water or unpolluted industrial or commercial process water stormwater and surface drainage stormwater and surface drainage shall be admitted to only such sewers as are specifically designated as storm sewers or storm drains unpolluted process and cooling waters may upon written application and approval by the approving authority be discharged to storm sewers or storm drains federal standards upon the promulgation of the federal categorical pretreatment standards for a particular industrial subcategory the federal standard shall immediately supersede those limitations imposed under this article that are less stringent than the federal standards upset or unauthorized discharge in the event of an upset or unauthorized discharge a written report must be submitted to the approving authority within five days and immediate phone notification is required to both the town and to dhec permission required to make connections the town shall reserve the right to inspect and grant or reject permission for all connections to the sewerage system and require payment of a tap fee before permission to connect can be granted to any person acceptable discharges a any waters or wastes discharged by any person which exceed the following characteristics may be admitted into the sanitary sewers conditionally 1 a fiveday bod greater than 250 parts per million by weight  or 2 containing suspended solids of more than 400 parts per million by weight b where necessary in the opinion of the approving authority the owner shall provide at his expense such preliminary handling or treatment as may be required to 1 reduce the bod to 250 parts per million by weight and the suspended solids to 400 parts per million by weight  or 2 change the objectionable characteristics or constituents to come within the maximum limited provided for in sections 1912 and 1915 c where the volume of any waters or wastes discharged by any person exceeds the limits set forth under section 1916 the entire volume of such wastes shall be understood to come within the limitations set forth under this section daily volume any water or wastes discharged by any person which have an average working day flow greater than 1000 gallons may be required to control the rules of discharge so as to prevent overloads preliminary treatment facilities a any waters or wastes exceeding the limits set forth under sections 1918 and 1919 or when necessary in the opinion of the approving authority the person shall provide at his own expense such preliminary handling as may be necessary to control the quality and rates of discharge of such waters or wastes over each 24hour period plans specifications and other pertinent information related to proposed preliminary treatment or handling facilities shall be submitted for the approval of the approving authority and no construction of such facilities shall be commenced until such approval is obtained in writing b the facilities shall be constructed in accordance with a compliance schedule submitted by the person and approved by the approving authority and within the time limitations as may be specified by the federal pretreatment regulations application to be made to the approving authority a any person who is now discharging any industrial wastes into the towns public sewers or who desires to discharge such wastes into the sewers shall make written application to the approving authority giving complete information as to the nature and characteristics of the waste as determined by an analysis of a composite sample of the waste made by an independent laboratory b any person having been granted authority by the approving authority to discharge industrial wastes into the towns public sewers and who shall change or cause to be changed the nature or quantity of such waste shall before making such change receive the approval of the approving authority of such change and shall also furnish the approving authority a complete analysis of a composite sample of the waste as determined by and independent laboratory c if such person or industry shall be located outside the corporate limits and is now discharging of should wish to make such connection and discharge such wastes as described above he shall make written application to the approving authority and shall furnish the approving authority a complete analysis of a composite sample of the waste as determined by an independent laboratory grease oil and sand interceptors grease oil and sand interceptors shall be provided when in the opinion of the approving authority they are necessary for the proper handling and control of liquid wastes containing grease oil or sand in excessive amounts such interceptors shall not be required for private living quarters or dwelling units but may be required for industrial or commercial establishments public eating places hospitals hotels abattoirs or other institutions such interceptors shall be readily accessible for cleaning and inspection and shall be maintained by the owner at his expense and in continuously efficient operation at all times storage tanks whenever the total volume of wastes to be discharged by any person in any one day shall exceed the limits set forth in section 1919 or where such wastes have considerable variation in pollutional value such person shall be required to construct holding or storage tanks in order to equalize the discharge of wastes over a 24hour period such tanks shall be equipped to thoroughly mix the waste so that its quality shall be uniform when discharged to the public sewers control of volume  notice of interruption a the control of the volume of the discharge of the wastes to the sewer shall be by a waterworkstype rate controller or other approved device the operation and setting of which shall be directed by the approving authority b notice shall be given the approving authority when normal operations of the industry will be interrupted for 24 hours or longer and wastes will not be available for discharge maintenance of preliminary treatment and holding facilities where preliminary treatment or holding facilities are provided for any purpose they shall be maintained continuously in satisfactory and effective operation by the owner at his own expense control manholes any person discharging industrial wastes into the public sewers may be required to construct and maintain a suitable control or inspection manhole either downstream from any treatment storage or other approved works or if pretreatment is not required at the point where the wastes enter the public sewers such manhole shall be located so as to be readily accessible and shall be constructed in such a manner as may be approved by the approving authority as to facilitate such inspection or measuring as may be necessary from proper sampling andor control of the waste discharged dilution prohibited no person shall ever increase the use of process water or in any way attempt to dilute a discharge as a partial or complete substitute for adequate treatment to achieve compliance with the requirements of sections 1912 and 1915 division 3  administration inspections the approving authority and duly authorized employees of the town shall be permitted to enter upon all properties for the purpose of inspection observation measurement sampling inspection and copying of records and testing in accordance with the provisions of this article the town shall notify if available a representative of the industry or person prior to entering the properties for purposes of this section records shall be defined as any and all documents related to the production treatment and discharge of wastewater to the towns sewer system tests and analyses all tests and analyses of the characteristics of sewage to which reference is made in this chapter shall be made in accordance with the procedures given in the federal register 40 cfr  such tests and analyses shall be determined at the control manhole provided for in section 1926 or at the point of discharge of any sewage at the site of its origin on the premises of any person discharging such sewage into the sewers measurement of flow a the volume of flow used in determining the total discharge of industrial wastes shall be based upon metered water consumption as shown in the records of meter readings maintained by the town in the event that a person discharging wastes into the public sewers produces evidence to the approving authority that more than ten percent of the total volume of water used for all purposes does not reach the public sewers then an estimate percentage of total water consumption to be used in determining industrial waste discharge may be agreed upon between the approving authority and the person discharging such industrial wastes into the public sewers b where any person discharging industrial wastes to the public sewers procures all or any part of his water supply form sources other than the water department of the town the person discharging the said wastes shall install and maintain at his expense water meters of a type approved by the approving authority for the purposes of determining the proper volume of industrial waste discharged to such sewers sampling  examination methods a the industrial waste of each person discharging wastes into the public sewers shall be subject to periodic inspection and a determination of character and concentration of such wastes shall be made quarterly or more often as may be deemed necessary by the approving authority or his authorized assistants such inspection and tests shall also be made immediately after any approved process change which may affect the quantity or quality of the waste discharged b sewage samples shall be collected in such manner as to representative of actual volume and quality of the waste the collection of samples shall be at the control manhole provided for in section 1926 or as specified in the industrys wastewater contribution permit procedures used in the collection of samples shall be those set forth in federal register 40 cfr c the determination of the flow character and concentration of industrial wastes as provided herein shall be used as a basis for charges cost recovery surcharges and compliance with sections 1912 and 1915 the person discharging industrial wastes shall be entitled to request a hearing in accordance with section 1962 to show cause why the results of such determination is not within accepted standards for precision and accuracy d all significant industrial users shall submit to the approving authority selfmonitoring reports indicating the nature and concentration of pollutants discharged to the sewer system the frequency of the monitoring and report requirements shall be as specified in the industrys wastewater contribution permit in the event selfmonitoring indicates a violation of any discharge limits as specified in the industrys wastewater contribution permit the industry must notify the approving authority within 24 hours resample and submit the results of both analyses within 30 days e the results of all tests and analyses performed by significant industrial users shall be reported to the approving authority connection of buildings to sewer main every building which is located within 200 feet of any sewer main operated and maintained by the town shall be connected thereto and shall utilize the same for wastewater disposal said connection shall be made prior to occupancy of any new building time limit for connection existing buildings which are provided with access as described in section 1932 shall connect to the seer main within a period of two years from date of completion of the sewer main  or at such time of failure or malfunction of existing waste disposal means  or at such time as directed by the county department of health upon notice that the existing means of waste disposal is a community health hazard and violation of federal state or local law septic tank system where no public sewer exists within the limitation of section 1932 or where connection is technically impractical the owner of such property may apply for a permit to construct and operate a septic tank system as approved by the county department of health and provided that the septic tank system is properly maintained so as to eliminate any hazard to the public health personnel for sewer system the town shall provide personnel to operate the system in number and skill as required by the rules and regulations of dhec the environmental protection agency epa and in conjunction with osha requirements use of storm sewers discharge of sanitary sewers into storm sewers shall be prohibited legal action by town if any person discharges sewage industrial wastes or other wastes into the towns sewage system contrary to the provisions of this article federal or state pretreatment requirements or any order of the town the town may commence an action for appropriate legal andor equitable relief in the court of the county division 4  wastewater contribution permit permit required all significant industrial users proposing to connect to or contribute to the sewage works shall obtain a wastewater contribution permit before connecting to or contributing to the sewage works application persons required to obtain a wastewater contribution permit shall complete and file with the town an application in the form prescribed by the town proposed new users shall apply at least 90 days prior to connecting to or contributing to the sewage works permit holders to comply with federal standards within nine months of the promulgation of a federal categorical pretreatment standard the wastewater contribution permit of persons subject to such standards shall be revised to require compliance with such standard within the time frame prescribed by such standard where a person subject to a federal categorical pretreatment standard has not previously submitted an application for a wastewater contribution permit as required under section 1938 the person shall apply for such permit within 180 days after the promulgation of the applicable federal categorical pretreatment standard permits subject to regulation wastewater contribution permits shall be expressly subject to all provisions of this article and all other applicable regulations user charges and fees established by the town permits may contain discharge limitations and conditions as deemed appropriate by the town to ensure compliance with this article discharge limitations and conditions may be more stringent than federal or state limitations and conditions if determined necessary to ensure compliance with all applicable federal state and local regulations length of validity of permit  conditions permits shall be issued for a specified time period not to exceed five years the user shall apply for permit reissuance a minimum of 180 days prior to the expiration date the conditions of the permit may be subject to modification by the town during the term of the permit as limitations or requirements identified in article ii are modified or other just cause exists the user shall be informed of any proposed changes in his permit at least 90 days prior to the effective date of change and be allowed to request modification any changes or new conditions in the permit shall include a reasonable time schedule for compliance transfer or sale of permit wastewater contribution permits are issued to a specific person for a specific operation a permit shall not be reassigned transferred or sold to a new owner new person different premises or a new or changed operation without the approval of the town any succeeding owner or person shall also comply with the terms and conditions of the existing permit confidential information a information and date on a person obtained form reports questionnaires permit applications permits and monitoring programs and from inspections shall be available to the public or other governmental agency without restriction unless the person specifically requests and is able to demonstrate to the satisfaction of the town that the release of such information would divulge information processes or methods of production entitled to protection as trade secrets of the person b when requested by the person furnishing the report the portions of a report which might disclose trade secrets or secret processes shall not be made available for inspection by the public but shall be made available upon written request to governmental agencies for uses related to this article the national pollutant discharge elimination system npdes permit state disposal system permit andor the pretreatment programs  provided however that such portions of a report shall be available for use by the state or any state agency in judicial review for enforcement proceedings involving the person furnishing the report wastewater constituents and characteristics will not be recognized as confidential information c information accepted by the town as confidential shall not be transmitted to any governmental agency or to the general public by the town unless a tenbusiness day notification is given to the person division 5  charges schedule of charges the town shall at least annually adopt an adequate schedule of sewer service charges to defray the cost of operating and maintaining the sanitary sewerage system the costs to be used as a basis for determining charges shall include but is not necessarily limited to direct operation and maintenance administration collection and billing of charges bond redemption studies and reports professional fees repairs capital improvements and depreciation the sewer service charges adopted shall be such that each user pays at least his proportionate share of all costs herein noted and nondiscriminatorily and uniformly applied notice of charges the sewer service charges shall be published in a form for public distribution by mail to each customers billing address and notice shall become a part of this article upon adoption and public notification and shall be based on the cost of treatment per 1000 gallons of sewage basis for charges  delinquent bills the approving authority shall levy monthly sewer service charges based on actual water consumption as obtained from water meter readings or other means as provided if the bill is not paid by the fifteenth of the second month following the date of billing the bill shall be delinquent and service discontinued sewer surcharge rates a surcharge covering the cost of treatment of excessive industrial wastes shall be determined in the following manner 1 the approving authority shall fix the rate to be charged during the new fiscal year at the beginning of said fiscal year for the excess bod of suspended solids from actual costs per 1000 pounds removed from the combined domestic and industrial wastes as experienced at the sewage treatment plant during the preceding year 2 the rate shall be applied to the amount of bod in excess of 250 ppm and suspended solids in excess of 400 ppm as determined by averaging at least three waste discharge samples 3 the surcharge rate shall be set at $015 per pound for bod removal and $014 per pound for tss removal septic waste charges a haulers of septic waste accepted at the towns wastewater treatment facility shall be charged a fee of $5000 per 1000 gallons of septic waste this fee must be prepaid to the town clerk before any septic waste can be disposed of in the towns wastewater treatment facility b only residential septic waste that contains no industrial waste toxins oil grease or other contaminants that would harm or damage in any way the equipment or treatment process of the towns wastewater treatment facility will be accepted by the town connection fees a connection fees to the towns sewer system shall be based upon size as determined by the following sewer connections inside town outoftown 4 $40000 $60000 b all sewer connections over four inches shall be charged at a rate equal to the towns actual costs of installation plus 20 percent for intown customers with a minimum charge of $100000 outoftown customers shall be charged a rate equal to the towns actual cost of installation plus 40 percent with a minimum charge of $200000 c apartments duplexes condominiums townhouses and motels on one connection shall be charged a connection fee in accordance with the connection size required or one connection fee per unit whichever is greater d mobile home parks on one connection shall be charged one connection fee for each mobile home space as provided in accordance with the above schedule e business or industrial users on one connection shall be charged a connection fee in accordance with the connection size required or one connection fee per unit whichever is greater f sewer connections made by any party other than the town of cheraw shall be charged an access fee of $7500 per unit sewer service charges a the sewer service charges shall be as follows per 1000 gallons volume intown outoftown industrial minimum 2000 gal $625 $1665  per 1000 gal 203 406 203  any customer who consistently uses in excess of 750000 gallons per month yearround b of the water and sewer system whose checks are returned for insufficient funds shall be charged a fee of $2500 division 6  sanitary sewer extensions developer to construct sewerage system construction of sanitary sewerage systems in any new development shall be the responsibility of any person performing such development plans and specifications all new development proposing to build sanitary sewers or extensions to existing sanitary sewers which will connect directly or indirectly into the towns sanitary sewerage system shall confirm its plans and specifications to requirement of the approving authority the plans and specifications shall be prepared by a registered engineer who is authorized by the laws of the state of south carolina and is approved or approvable by any and all local county and state authorities having jurisdiction approval procedure approval of systems shall be accomplished in accordance with the following procedures 1 submit preliminary construction plans to the approving authority in sufficient detail to indicate location system layout line sizes service connections flows character of sewage relationship with a connection to the towns system or other disposal system 2 receive preliminary approval form town and other jurisdictional agencies 3 prepare construction drawings and documents for towns approval 4 secure all other agency approval of construction drawings and contract documents 5 upon receipt of all approvals proceed with construction notifying the approving authority of construction schedules 6 provide the approving authority and its authorized representatives with permission for onsite inspection during construction 7 upon completion of construction the engineer employed by the development shall inspect and furnish to the approving authority at no cost to the town his certificate of completion indicating that the subject sewerage system has been constructed in accordance with the approved plans and specifications and shall provide four copies of as constructed drawings sanitary sewers conveyed to town sanitary sewers constructed within new developments may be conveyed to the town provided all such sewers are located within public rightsofway or easements of adequate widths to provide maintenance vehicle access conveyance procedure sewerage systems to be conveyed to the town will be done by the owner preparing and submitting to the town an instrument of conveyance conveying the constructed system to the town at no cost to the town and the system shall thereafter be owned operated and maintained by the town as provided for in this article the instrument of conveyance shall also include permanent easements and rightsofway fully described and duly recorded at the appropriate authority warranty required the owner or his authorized agent shall submit a warranty which is a legal instrument in which the owner warrants the material equipment and construction of the system for 12 months the owner shall further warrant to the approving authority that all fees have been paid by him such that there is no outstanding indebtedness remaining and holding the town harmless in each instance sewer taps all sewer taps shall be made during the construction from the main out to the property line location of all taps shall be recorded on the as constructed drawings compatibility with town plans all sewerage extensions must be compatible with present and future plans and needs of the town use of old sewers old building sewers may not be used in connection with service to new buildings unless it can be proven that the materials meet all of the requirements for a suitable installation division 7  enforcement administrative enforcement remedies a notice of violation whenever the town finds that any person has violated or is violating this division a wastewater contribution permit or order issued hereunder the town may serve upon said person written notice of violation within ten days of the receipt date of this notice an explanation of the violation and a plan for the satisfactory correction and prevention thereof to include specific required actions shall be submitted to the town submission of this plan in no way relieves the person of liability for any violation occurring before or after receipt of the notice of violation b consent orders the town is hereby empowered to enter into consent orders assurances of voluntary compliance or other similar documents establishing an agreement with the person responsible for the noncompliance such orders will include specific actions to be taken by the person to correct the noncompliance within a time period also specified by the order consent orders shall have the same force and effect as administrative orders issued pursuant to paragraph d below c show cause hearing the town may order any person which causes or contributes to violation of this division or wastewater contribution permit or order issued hereunder to show cause why a proposed enforcement action should not be taken notice shall be served on the person specifying the time and place for the meeting the proposed enforcement action and the reasons of such action and a request that the user show cause why this proposed enforcement action should not be taken the notice of this meeting shall be served personally or by registered or certified mail at least ten days prior to the hearing such notice may be served on any principal executive general partner or corporate officer whenever or not a duly notified person appears as noticed immediate enforcement action may be pursued d compliance order when the town finds that a person has violated or continues to violate this division or a permit or order issued hereunder the town may issue any order to the person responsible for the discharge directing that following a specified timer period sewer service shall be discontinued unless adequate treatment facilities devices or other related appurtenances have been installed and are properly operated orders may also contain such other requirements as might be reasonably necessary and appropriate to address the noncompliance including the installation of pretreatment technology additional selfmonitoring and management practices e cease and desist orders when the town finds that a person has violated or continues to violate this division or a permit or order issued hereunder the town may issue an order to cease and desist all such violations as may be needed to respond to a continuing or threatened violation including halting operations and terminating the discharge f emergency suspensions the town may suspend the wastewater treatment service andor wastewater contribution permit of a person whenever such suspension is necessary in order to stop an actual or threatened discharge presenting or causing an imminent or substantial endangerment to the health or welfare of persons the potw or the environment g disconnection of service for nonpayment of bills the town shall disconnect sewer service for any person who is more than 90 days in arrears with payment of monthly sewer service charges except as provided in sections 1945 reconnection may be permitted after payment of all charges and penalties as herein provided suspension of service  appeal procedure this section shall be identical to that stated in subsection 1962c hereinabove publication of violators the town shall annually publish in the largest paper of general circulation a list of persons who were in significant noncompliance of applicable categorical pretreatment requirements or standards at least once during the previous 12month period falsifying information any person who knowingly makes any false statements representation or certification in any application record report plan or other document filed or required to be maintained pursuant to this article or who falsifies tampers with or knowingly renders inaccurate any monitoring device or method required under this article shall upon conviction be punished by a fine as provided in section 1966 penalty any person who is found to have violated an order of the town council or have willfully or negligently failed to comply with any provision of this article and the orders rules regulations and permits issued hereunder shall be fined up to $100000 each day on which a violation shall occur or continue shall be deemed a separate and distinct offense in addition to the penalties provided herein the town may recover reasonable attorneys fees court costs court reporters fees and other expenses of litigation by appropriate suit at law against the person found to have violated this article or the orders rules regulations and permits issued hereunder article iii  drought management and response plan application the following drought management and response plans shall apply to all industries commercial institutional entities and individuals in the incorporated and unincorporated area served by the town of cheraw this drought management plan outlines the framework by which the town of cheraw will internally prepare for potential water shortages the drought response plan provides regulations by which the town will manage and control its customer water usage during various levels of a drought situation adoption of drought management plan the town council hereby adopts the cheraw drought management plan the plan may be amended from time to time as necessary provided that such changes are consistent with polices and procedures adopted by the state of south carolina definition of terms for the purpose of the management plan and the response plan the following definitions shall apply aesthetic water use water use for ornamental or decorative purposes such as fountains reflecting pools waterfalls etc commercial and industrial use water uses integral to the production of goods andor services by any establishment having profit as its primary aim conservation reduction in water use to prevent depletion or waste of the resource customer any person company or organization using finished water owned or supplied by the town of cheraw domestic water use water use for personal needs or for household purposes such as drinking bathing cooking sanitation or for cleaning a residence business industry or institution drought alert phases there are four drought alert phases to be determined by the drought response committee for the state of south carolina the four phases are 1 incipient drought 2 moderate drought 3 severe drought 4 extreme drought drought response management areas in order to prevent overly broad response to drought conditions drought response measures shall be considered within individual drought management areas or within individual counties there are four drought management areas corresponding to the major river basins in south carolina the four areas are 1 west or savannah 2 central or santee 3 northeast or pee dee 4 southern or ashepoo combahee and edisto drought response committee a committee composed of state and local representatives created for the purpose of coordinating responses to water supply shortages with drought management areas and making recommendations for action to the south carolina department of natural resources andor the governor the committee is composed of state agency representatives from the south carolina emergency management division of the office of the adjutant general south carolina department of health and environmental control south carolina department of agriculture south carolina forestry commission and the south carolina department of natural resources as well as local committees representing counties municipalities public service districts private water suppliers agriculture industry domestic users regional councils of government commissions of public works power generation facilities special purpose districts and soil and water conservation districts essential water use water used specifically for fire fighting maintaining instream flow requirements to satisfy federal state or local public health and safety requirements finished water water distributed after treatment the terms water use water user and water customer refer to finished water use unless otherwise defined institutional water use water used by government public and private educational institutions churches and places of worship water utilities and organizations within the public domain mgd million gallons per day nonessential water use categories of water use other than essential water use examples of nonessential water use include landscape irrigation and the washing of buildings parking lots automobiles etc residential equivalent unit reu an equivalency unit defined to be equal to one singlefamily residence the town of cheraws allocated water capacity equals 300 gallons per reu sc department of natural resources the state agency with primacy to implement the provisions of the drought response act of 2000 water supply shortage lack of adequate available water caused by drought to meet normal demands drought management plan a introduction to ensure that the town of cheraw adequately manages its water system during droughtrelated conditions an organized plan is necessary for system operation and reliability proper communications effective coordination and ultimate allocation of water use prior planning will complement the towns ability to respond to drought conditions and to enforce the related drought response plan b designation of water system drought response representative administering a drought plan requires an individual with the skills necessary to undertake a comprehensive public information program and the judgment to deal with equity issues arising from enforcement of a mandatory program the drought response representative from the town will be the towns public utility director c description of water system layout water sources capacities and yields 1 the town of cheraw is located in the pee dee drought response management area of south carolina the system serves most customers within the municipality and one subdivision outside 2 the town operates a 45 mgd water treatment facility the ground finish water storage is 075 mg there are four elevated storage tanks in the system with a total capacity of 175 mg 3 the system services 6500 customers water taps the transmission lines are 16 inches inches that are connected directions 4 the water source available to the system is the great pee dee river 5 the scdhec total permitted capacity of the water system is 45 mgd d identification of specific drought or water shortage indicators certain historical trends provide valuable indicators of a systems ability to meet demand when demand begins to outpace supply the town of cheraw has developed certain triggers for use during drought or demand water shortages that describe when specific phases of the drought response ordinance are implemented the specific triggers are as follows moderate drought phase river level is 18 inches at the raw water intake for three consecutive days severe drought phase the river level is less than 12 inches at the intake for three consecutive days extreme drought phase the river level is less than eight inches at the intake for three consecutive days e cooperative agreements and alternate water supply sources 1 successful drought management requires a comprehensive program by the water utility agreements with other water purveyors may be necessary for alternative water supply sources the town of cheraw presently has an agreement with the chesterfield county rural water company whereby the town can receive or provide water to the rural water company during certain drought periods 2 the town will consider other mutual agreements with appropriate water purveyors as needed f predrought planning efforts before the occurrence of a water supply shortage and the need to implement the emergency provisions of this article it is important that certain preresponse measures be taken with the aim of conserving the systems source water as well as the water distributed to the customer the town of cheraw has taken the following such actions 1 identification of all major water users of the system carolina canners crown cork & seal co ina usa stanley tools and highland industries 2 identification of all users with whom there are conservation agreements all users are subject to the town ordinance this article concerning conservation during drought periods 3 a vigorous public education program is critical for achieving substantial water use reductions an effective public outreach program will keep the public informed of the water supply situation what actions will mitigate drought emergency problems and how well the public is doing in terms of meeting the program goals keeping the public involved informed and participating in the decisionmaking process is key to implementing an effective drought management plan the town uses the following public newspapers to advise the public of drought problems the cheraw chronicle the chesterfield shopper the link and the progressive 4 the town has installed meters on all of the towns properties in order to account for all water uses g capital planning and investment for system reliability and demand forecasting capital improvements strongly enhance the ability of the water utility system to manage during times of drought the utility must provide for system operation flexibility improved pumping and storage capacity and new technologies to meet future demands the towns current capital improvement program includes the following 1 installation of a water line between cheraw and chesterfield both towns have the ability to use the other for an emergency water backup source the chesterfield county rural water company is also tied into this line 2 the town is reviewing the possibility of locating a well that can be used as an alternate water source proclamation of drought phases a moderate drought phase upon notification by the south carolina drought response committee that a moderate drought response condition is present and is expected to persist andor upon determination by the town of cheraw that a moderate water supply shortage exists based on certain trigger levels the town will seek voluntary reductions from its customers in the use of water for all purposes and voluntary reductions on the use of water during peak water demand periods specifically the goal during this phase is to achieve a reduction of 20 percent in residential water use and 15 percent in other water uses such as commercial industrial institutional and irrigation and a reduction in overall water use of 15 percent to accomplish this the town of cheraw will take the following actions 1 issue a proclamation to be released to the local media town of cheraw customers and to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center that moderate drought conditions are present 2 provide written notification to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center and routinely publish in a newspaper of general circulation in the service area of the water system the voluntary conservation measures that the customers are being requested to follow during moderate drought conditions including a reduce residential water use to 65 gallons per person per day and a maximum of 200 gallons per household per day  b eliminate the washing down of sidewalks walkways driveways parking lots tennis courts and other hardsurfaced areas  c eliminate the washing down of buildings for purposes other than immediate fire protection  d eliminate the flushing of gutters  e eliminate the domestic washing of motorbikes boats cars etc  f eliminate the use of water to maintain fountains reflective ponds and decorative water bodies for aesthetic or scenic purposes except where necessary to support aquatic life  g reduce watering of lawns plants trees gardens shrubbery and flora on private or public property to the minimum necessary encourage outdoor watering to be done during offpeak hours  h reduce the amount of water obtained from fire hydrants for construction purposes fire drills or for any other purposes other than fire fighting or flushing necessary to maintain water quality  and i limit normal water use by commercial and individual customers including but not limited to the following 1 stop serving water in addition to another beverage routinely in restaurants  2 stop maintaining water levels in scenic and recreational ponds and lakes except for the minimum amount required to support aquatic life  3 cease water service to customers who have been given a tenday notice to repair one or more leaks and have failed to do so 3 intensify maintenance efforts to identify and correct water leaks throughout the distribution system 4 cease to install new irrigation taps on the water system 5 continue to encourage and educate customers to comply with voluntary water conservation b severe drought phase upon notification by the sc drought response committee that a moderate drought response condition is present and is expected to persist andor upon determination by the town of cheraw that a moderate water supply shortage exists based on certain trigger levels the town will seek voluntary reduction in the use of water for all purposes and mandatory restrictions on nonessential usage and restrictions on times when certain water usage is allowed specifically the goal during this phase is to achieve a reduction of 25 percent in residential water use 20 percent in all other water use categories and reduction on overall water use of 20 percent to accomplish these goals the town will take the following actions 1 issue a proclamation to be released to the local media town of cheraw customers and to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center that severe drought conditions are present 2 provide written notification to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center and routinely publish in a newspaper of general circulation in the service area of the water system the voluntary conservation measures and mandatory restrictions to be placed on the use of water supplied by the utility including a voluntary reduction of residential water use by the utilitys customers to 55 gallons per person per day and a maximum of 170 gallons per household per day  b control landscape irrigation by the utilitys customers by staggering watering times  c mandatory restrictions on the use of water supplied by the utility for activities including 1 eliminate the washing down of sidewalks walkways driveways parking lots tennis courts and other hard surfaced areas  2 eliminate the washing down of buildings for purposes other than immediate fire protection  3 eliminate the flushing of gutters  4 eliminate the domestic washing of motorbikes boats cars etc  5 eliminate the use of water to maintain fountains reflective ponds and decorative water bodies for aesthetic or scenic purposes except where necessary to support aquatic life  6 eliminate filling or maintaining public or private swimming pools  7 eliminate obtaining water from fire hydrants for construction purposes fire drills or for any other purposes other than fire fighting or flushing necessary to maintain water quality d limit normal water use by commercial and individual customers including but not limited to the following 1 stop serving water in addition to another beverage routinely in restaurants  2 stop maintaining water levels in scenic and recreational ponds and lakes except for the minimum amount required to support aquatic life  3 limit irrigating golf courses and any portion of its grounds  4 cease water service to customers who have been given a tenday notice to repair one or more leaks and have failed to do so  5 limit expanding commercial nursery facilities placing new agricultural land in production or planting or landscaping when required by site design review process 3 intensify maintenance efforts to identify and correct water leaks throughout the distribution system 4 continue to cease installation of new irrigation taps on the water system 5 publicize widely the penalties to be imposed for violations of mandatory restrictions and the procedures to be followed if a variance in the restriction is requested 6 expand the use of education and public relations efforts and emphasize the penalties associated with violating the mandatory restrictions 7 provide written notification to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center regarding the success of the voluntary and mandatory restrictions c extreme drought phase upon notification by the drought response committee that an extreme drought response condition is present and is expected to persist andor upon determination by the town of cheraw that a severe water supply shortage exists based on certain trigger levels the town will seek voluntary reduction in the use of water for all purposes and mandatory restrictions on nonessential usage and restrictions on times when certain water usage is allowed specifically the goal during this phase is to achieve a reduction of 30 percent in residential water use 25 percent in all other water use categories and reduction in overall water use of 25 percent to accomplish these goals the town will take the following actions 1 issue a proclamation to be released to the local media town of cheraw customers and to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center that severe drought conditions are present 2 provide written notification to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center and routinely publish in a newspaper of general circulation in the service area the mandatory restrictions to be placed on the use of water supplied by the utility including a limiting residential water use by the utilitys customers to 50 gallons per person per day and a maximum of 150 gallons per household per day b eliminate landscape irrigation by all customers c mandatory restrictions on the use of water supplied by the utility for activities including 1 eliminate the washing down of sidewalks walkways driveways parking lots tennis courts and other hard surfaced areas  2 eliminate the washing down of buildings for purposes other than immediate fire protection  3 eliminate the flushing of gutters  4 no domestic washing of motorbikes boats cars etc  5 eliminate the use of water to maintain fountains reflective ponds and decorative water bodies for aesthetic or scenic purposes except where necessary to support aquatic life  6 eliminate filling or maintaining public or private swimming pools  7 eliminate obtaining water from fire hydrants for construction purposes fire drills or for any other purposes other than fire fighting or flushing necessary to maintain water quality d limit normal water use by commercial and individual customers including but not limited to the following 1 stop serving water in addition to another beverage routinely in restaurants  2 stop maintaining water levels in scenic and recreational ponds and lakes except for the minimum amount required to support aquatic life  3 limit irrigating golf courses and any portion of its grounds  4 cease water service to customers who have been given a tenday notice to repair one or more leaks and have failed to do so  5 limit expanding commercial nursery facilities placing new agricultural land in production or planting or landscaping when required by site design review process 3 intensify maintenance efforts to identify and correct water leaks throughout the distribution system 4 continue to cease installation of new irrigation taps on the water system 5 outline other conservation measures examples include a place a moratorium on the issuance of all new water service connections and contracts for all new water main extensions as part of the public information process provide notice to developers of the moratorium b encourage all residential water customers to voluntarily reduce overall monthly water usage to 70% percent of the customers monthly average if voluntary reduction of usage is not successful the town may at its option implement the following excessive use rate schedule for water tier i 0225 gallonsreu regular water rate tier ii 226500 gallonsreu 2 times regular rate tier iii over 500 gallonsreu 3 times regular rate c if the conservation measures of the ordinance or plan prove inadequate to mitigate the effects of the drought conditions or water supply availability the town may take additional actions including but not limited to the following 1 increasing the gallonreu limits in the different tiers  2 reduction of water pressure as needed 6 publicize widely the penalties to be imposed for violations of mandatory restrictions and the procedures to be followed if a variance in the restrictions is requested 7 expand the use of education and public relations efforts as conducted under the moderate and severe drought status and emphasize the penalties associated with violating the mandatory restrictions 8 provide written notification monthly to the south carolina department of natural resources drought information center regarding the success of the mandatory restrictions rationing if a drought threatens the protection of public health and safety the town is hereby authorized to ration the availability of water enforcement of restrictions if any customer of the town of cheraw fails to comply with the mandatory water use restrictions of this article the customer shall be given a written notice of such failure to comply which cites the date of said violation and shall be assessed surcharges in accordance with the following schedule first violation a $2500 surcharge shall be added to the customers water bill second violation an additional $5000 surcharge shall be added to the customers water bill third violation the customers water service shall be terminated and restored only after payment of a surcharge of $10000 in addition to the previously assessed surcharges law enforcement agencies and other authorized agencies or designated employees in the respective jurisdiction which is being supplied water by the town of cheraw shall diligently enforce the provisions of the drought response ordinance variances a customers who in their belief are unable to comply with the mandatory water use restrictions of this drought response ordinance may petition for a variance from restrictions by filing a petition with the cheraw town clerk within ten working days after issuance of the proclamation requiring water use restrictions b all petitions for variance shall contain the following information 1 name and address of the petitioner 2 purpose of water usage 3 special provision from which the petitioner is requesting relief 4 detailed statement as to how the curtailment declaration adversely affects the petitioner 5 description of the relief desired 6 period of time for which the variance is sought 7 economic value of the water use 8 damage or harm to the petitioner or others if the petitioner complies with this article 9 restrictions with which the petitioner is expected to comply and the compliance date 10 steps the petitioner is taking to meet the restrictions from which the variance is sought and the expected date of compliance 11 other information as needed c in order for the variance to be granted the petitioner must demonstrate clearly that compliance with this article cannot be technically accomplished during the duration of the water supply shortage without having an adverse impact upon the best interests of the community d in addition the town is authorized to grant temporary variances for existing water uses otherwise prohibited under this article if it is determined that failure to grant such variance should cause an emergency condition adversely affecting health sanitation and fire protection for the public no such variance shall be retroactive or otherwise justify any violation of this article occurring prior to the issuance of the variance variances granted by the town shall include a timetable for compliance and shall expire when the water supply shortage no longer exists unless the petitioner has failed to meet specific requirements wrecker services article i  in general compliance required the following regulations in this chapter shall be adhered to by all wrecker services utilized by the cheraw police department removal from rotation list failure of any wrecker service to comply with the regulations as stated may result in their removal from the cheraw police departments wrecker rotation list by the police chief or the town administrator article ii  requirements financial interest of police officer prohibited no cheraw police officer shall hold any financial interest or any form of ownership interest in any wrecker service location within town limits  license any wrecker service which wishes to be placed on the police departments wrecker rotation list must have a business physically located within the municipal limits of the town and must have an appropriate valid business license availability wrecker services shall be available to the police department and the public on a 24hour basis storage area the wrecker service shall maintain a safe storage area for all vehicles towed this may be a locked building or a secured fencedin area where the stored vehicle and other property shall not be accessible to the public equipment a all wreckers shall be equipped with legally authorized lighting and other safety equipment to protect the motoring public such equipment shall be maintained in good working order b equipment such as brooms shovels etc must be carried on all wreckers whereby to remove glass and other debris from the highway the highway shall be cleaned by the wrecker service prior to leaving the scene of any accident c the wrecker service must have equipment of sufficient size to handle a disabled vehicle including a rollback truck to accommodate those vehicles unable to be towed any additional equipment specified by the south carolina highway patrol for wrecker services by statutory authority under sc laws  5666180 must also be maintained by those wrecker services on the towns wrecker rotation list signs each wrecker service on the rotation list must place a sign on the door of each of its wreckers indicating the name address and telephone number of the service this sign shall be painted on or otherwise permanently affixed to the door of the wrecker the letters of the sign must be no less than two inches high if the wrecker is registered in a name other than that of the wrecker service the owners name must also appear on the door in letters no less than oneinch high all lettering on wreckers shall be plainly visible and shall be in a color which contrasts to that of the wrecker liability insurance a any wrecker service on the rotation list shall carry liability insurance on its wreckers and its premises in an amount no less than $10000000 and must submit evidence of such insurance to the town clerk b any wrecker service on the rotation list shall carry garage keepers liability insurance covering customers vehicles in an amount not less than $2500000 and must submit evidence of such insurance to the town clerk charges charges for work performed must be reasonable article iii  procedures administration of list the wrecker rotation list shall be administered fairly and in a manner designed to insure that all wrecker services on the list have equal opportunity to the towing business arising from the rotation list solicitation from highway wrecker services and operators shall be familiar with and shall comply with the laws regarding solicitation form the highway response upon police request wreckers shall only respond upon request of the proper police authority response under any other condition may result in removal from the wrecker rotation list owner of vehicle to choose service unless the owner or driver of a vehicle is incapacitated or unavailable the owner or driver of a wrecked or disabled vehicle shall have the right to the wrecker service of his choice before calling any wrecker service to tow a wrecked or disabled vehicle the investigating officer on the scene if practical shall determine the owners or drivers preference of wrecker services and the wrecker service designated by the owner or drive shall be called time limit for service requested by owner any wrecker service which is not on rotation and that is requested to respond to the scene of an accident by the owner or operator of a disabled or wrecked vehicle may respond when requested so long as the wrecker responds within 15 minutes from the time it is notified recommendation by police prohibited in no event shall any cheraw police officer recommend any wrecker services to the owner of a wrecked or disabled vehicle nor shall any police officer ever recommend the services of any particular wrecker service in the performance of his duties unavailability when a wrecker service or wrecker driver is unable to answer a call police shall be promptly notified to that fact and the reason for the unavailability response time  notification of next service if a wrecker service does not respond within 15 minutes the dispatcher shall notify the second wrecker service which shall not lose its place in rotation any wrecker failing to respond within this time period on three separate occasions within a 12month period will automatically be removed from the rotation list when several cars involved in accident when two or more vehicles are involved in an accident the police officer on the scene will assign each wrecker a specific vehicle to be towed unless the owner or driver of such vehicle has a preference for a particular wrecker service assistance from other wrecker services a wrecker service may secure assistance form other wrecker services when necessary to do the job only one bill is to be submitted to the owner or operator of the towed vehicle for the work performed conduct of wrecker operators wrecker operators must conduct themselves in a proper manner in all accident scenes and in a proper manner when dealing with the public wrecker operator to secure personal property each wrecker service shall be responsible for securing personal property in a vehicle in an accident scene as best it can and the service shall be responsible for reasonably attempting to preserve personal property in a vehicle which is about to be towed from an accident scene in no event however shall a wrecker service be responsible for personal items which do not come into the possession of the wrecker service complaints involving police any complaints from wrecker services regarding any incidents involving the police department or its operation of the wrecker rotation list must be received by the police chief within 30 days of the alleged incident zoning regulations adoption by reference the zoning rules and regulations established by as contained in a separate zoning document are adopted by reference and made a definitions  107 5 | c h e r a w z o n i n g o r d i n a n c e enactment and jurisdiction 11 title these regulations shall be known and may be cited as the zoning cheraw south carolina 12 authority pursuant to the authority conferred by the general statues of south carolina 1976 laws title 6 of the comprehensive planning enabling act of 199 as amended the town of cheraw does ordain and enact into law the following articles and sections 13 purpose this intended to guide development in accordance with existing and future land use needs of the community and in accordance with the adopted comprehensive plan these regulations have been made in order to 1 protect promote and improve the public health safety morals convenience order prosperity and general welfare  2 guard and preserve the visual appearance of the community  3 lessen congestion in the streets  4 secure safety from fire  5 provide adequate air and light 6 prevent the overcrowding of land 7 avoid undue concentration of the population 8 protect and preserve historic and architecturally valuable structures and districts  9 facilitate the adequate provision of transportation water sewerage schools parks and other public improvements  and 10 conserve the value of property to accomplish the goals these regulations set forth requirements for 1 the location size placement use and occupancy of land and buildings  2 the creation of districts for the above purposes   3 methods of administration amendment and appeal of these regulations  4 the duties of the planning commission and board of appeals in the above regard  5 the provision of penalties for violation of these regulations  6 certain other legal requirements related to the exercise of planning powers 14 jurisdiction the regulations set forth herein shall apply to all land and improvements thereon within the boundaries of the town of cheraw south carolina and areas annexed thereto 6 | c h e r a w z o n i n g o r d i n a n c e establishment of districts and zoning map 21 establishment of districts for the purposes of these regulations the town of cheraw is hereby divided into the following districts table 21 zoning districts residential residential nc neighborhood commercial m1 manufacturing hc historic district r1 single family and duplex high density residential mc market commercial os  open space  conservation r2 multi family cc core commercial gw gateways gc general commercial 22 district boundaries established by zoning map the boundaries of the zoning districts are hereby established as shown on the map and titled official zoning map of the town of cheraw south carolina which together with all explanatory matter thereon is hereby adopted by reference and declared to be a part of this ordinance 23 official zoning map at least one copy of the official zoning map shall be maintained in the office of the town clerk search official zoning map shall be a tested by the town clerk and shall be available at all times for official zoning map search changes shall be entered on the official zoning map promptly after the amendment has been approved by the town council no ordinance amendment which involves matters portrayed on the official zoning map shall become effective until after such changes have been made on said map 7 | c h e r a w z o n i n g o r d i n a n c e no change of any nature shall be made on considered a violation of this ordinance and punished as provided by law regardless of the existence of purported copies of the official zoning map which may from time to time be made or published the
